Development Rules
✅ CORE RULES (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
1.	No file should exceed ~200 lines (except auto-generated files).
2.	One feature = one folder.
3.	Each feature owns its logic, UI, styles, and API calls.
4.	No feature directly touches another feature’s internals.
5.	Shared things go only into shared/.
6.	Future updates must follow this same pattern (no shortcuts).
________________________________________
📁 RECOMMENDED REACT PROJECT STRUCTURE
src/
│
├── app/                    # App bootstrapping
│   ├── App.jsx
│   ├── routes.jsx
│   └── providers.jsx
│
├── features/               # MAIN FEATURES (MOST IMPORTANT)
│   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── components/
│   │   │   └── LoginForm.jsx
│   │   ├── pages/
│   │   │   └── LoginPage.jsx
│   │   ├── hooks/
│   │   │   └── useAuth.js
│   │   ├── services/
│   │   │   └── authApi.js
│   │   ├── authSlice.js
│   │   └── index.js
│   │
│   ├── dashboard/
│   │   ├── components/
│   │   │   └── StatsCard.jsx
│   │   ├── pages/
│   │   │   └── DashboardPage.jsx
│   │   ├── hooks/
│   │   │   └── useDashboard.js
│   │   ├── services/
│   │   │   └── dashboardApi.js
│   │   └── index.js
│   │
│   ├── students/
│   │   ├── components/
│   │   ├── pages/
│   │   ├── hooks/
│   │   ├── services/
│   │   └── index.js
│
├── shared/                 # REUSABLE ACROSS FEATURES
│   ├── components/
│   │   ├── Button.jsx
│   │   └── Modal.jsx
│   ├── hooks/
│   │   └── useDebounce.js
│   ├── utils/
│   │   └── formatDate.js
│   ├── constants/
│   │   └── roles.js
│   └── styles/
│       └── theme.css
│
├── store/                  # GLOBAL STATE
│   ├── index.js
│   └── rootReducer.js
│
├── services/               # APP-LEVEL SERVICES
│   ├── apiClient.js
│   └── socket.js
│
├── config/
│   └── env.js
│
└── index.jsx
________________________________________
🧩 WHAT EACH FOLDER MEANS (SIMPLE EXPLANATION)
🔹 app/
Handles startup logic only
•	routing
•	providers (Redux, Context, Theme)
❌ No business logic here
________________________________________
🔹 features/ (MOST IMPORTANT)
Each folder = one real feature
Examples:
•	auth
•	dashboard
•	students
•	teachers
•	billing
•	reports
Each feature contains:
•	UI
•	logic
•	API calls
•	state (if needed)
This means:
👉 You can delete a feature without breaking the app
👉 Debugging is localized
👉 Teams can work independently
________________________________________
🔹 Inside a Feature Folder
students/
├── components/     # Small UI pieces
├── pages/          # Full pages
├── hooks/          # Feature logic
├── services/       # API calls
├── studentsSlice.js
└── index.js
✅ This makes it crystal-clear where anything belongs.
________________________________________
🔹 shared/
Anything reused in 2+ features
•	Buttons
•	Modals
•	Hooks
•	Utility functions
❌ No feature-specific logic allowed here
________________________________________
🔹 services/
Global services only:
•	Axios instance
•	WebSocket
•	Notifications
•	Logging
________________________________________
📜 STRICT NAMING CONVENTIONS
Item	Rule
Components	PascalCase.jsx
Hooks	useSomething.js
Services	somethingApi.js
Pages	SomethingPage.jsx
Redux	featureSlice.js
________________________________________
🔐 IMPORT RULE (VERY IMPORTANT)
❌ BAD:
import LoginForm from '../../features/auth/components/LoginForm'
✅ GOOD:
import { LoginForm } from '@/features/auth'
Every feature must export from its index.js.
________________________________________
🧠 WHY THIS ARCHITECTURE IS POWERFUL
•	Easy debugging
•	Clean Git history
•	Scales to 100+ features
•	Junior-friendly
•	Prevents “spaghetti code”
•	Perfect for long-term projects like school systems, SaaS, dashboards
________________________________________
🚦 FUTURE UPDATE RULE
Any new feature must:
1.	Get its own folder in features/
2.	Follow the same internal structure
3.	Never add logic directly into App.jsx
4.	Never exceed 200 lines per file

🏫 NDOVERA SCHOOL – COMPLETE SYSTEM BLUEPRINT
NDOVERA is a multi-tenant, offline-first, role-based, AI-assisted school operating system covering academics, administration, finance, communication, and appreciation (farming mode).
________________________________________
1️⃣ CORE SYSTEM PRINCIPLES
🔐 Single Source of Truth
•	CA Score Sheet → only source for results
•	Attendance Engine → only source for attendance
•	Fee Ledger → only source for fees
•	Role Assignments → determine access, not identity
🌐 Offline-First
•	Attendance
•	CA score entry
•	Messaging drafts
•	Tuck shop sales
•	Sync automatically when internet returns
🧩 Multi-Tenant
•	One parent → many children
•	Children → many schools
•	Staff → many roles
•	One login → role switching via ID Manager
________________________________________
2️⃣ 🆔 IDENTITY & ROLE ENGINE (ID MANAGER)
Think of the ID Manager as the digital identity card and control center for every person in the school system — staff, students, parents, and owners.
It answers three questions instantly:
1.	Who is this person?
2.	What roles do they have?
3.	What are they allowed to do right now?
________________________________________
📍 WHERE THIS LIVES IN THE SYSTEM
🔹 Location
•	Always visible in the top-right corner of the dashboard (like a profile icon)
•	Accessible from:
o	Web
o	Mobile app
o	Tablet (school office, class, clinic, etc.)
Clicking the profile opens the Smart ID Card.
________________________________________
🎴 SMART ID CARD (DIGITAL)
This is not just a profile picture — it is a live, interactive ID card.
🟦 FRONT OF THE CARD (Default View)
Looks like a real school ID card:
•	👤 Full Name
•	🖼 Profile Photo
•	🏫 School(s) the person belongs to
(important for owners, teachers, and admins managing multiple schools)
•	🟢 Status Badge
o	Active
o	Inactive
o	Locked
This side answers:
👉 “Who is this person?”
________________________________________
🔁 BACK OF THE CARD (Flip Animation)
When the card is tapped or clicked, it flips like a real card.
The back shows power and responsibility.
Shows:
•	🎓 All roles assigned
•	📋 What each role is responsible for
•	🔘 “Switch Role” button
This side answers:
👉 “What can this person do right now?”
________________________________________
🔘 SWITCH ROLE BUTTON (VERY IMPORTANT)
If a person has multiple roles, they must choose one at a time.
Example:
•	A teacher who is also HOD and Parent
•	An owner who is also Accountant
•	A principal who teaches a class
They tap Switch Role, choose one role, and the entire dashboard changes to match that role.
👉 This prevents:
•	Accidental misuse of power
•	Confusion
•	Security abuse
________________________________________
🧑‍🏫 ROLES SUPPORTED (EXPLAINED SIMPLY)
🎓 ACADEMIC ROLES
Role	What they do
Teacher	Teaches subjects
Class Teacher	Manages one class
HOD	Oversees a department
HOD Assistant	Helps the HOD
________________________________________
🏫 LEADERSHIP ROLES
Role	What they do
Principal	Leads academics & discipline
Head Teacher	Manages primary section
Nursery Head	Manages nursery section
➡️ Leadership focuses on learning, not money
________________________________________
🛠 OPERATIONS ROLES
Role	What they do
Librarian	Manages books & borrowing
Tuckshop Manager	Manages food sales
Transport Manager	Manages buses & drivers
Clinic Officer	Handles student health
➡️ They never see grades or finances unless allowed
________________________________________
🧾 ADMIN ROLES
Role	What they do
Accountant	Handles fees & expenses
HoS	Oversees school operations
Owner	School proprietor (tenant level)
Ami	Highest hidden system authority
🔐 Why “Ami” instead of “Super Admin”?
•	Attackers guess “admin” or “superadmin”
•	“Ami” is obscure, neutral, and unguessable
•	Only system creators know it exists
________________________________________
👥 USER ROLES
Role	What they do
Student	Learns
Parent	Views child progress
________________________________________
🔁 ROLE RULES (WHY THEY EXIST)
1️⃣ No Staff Without Responsibility
Every staff must:
•	Have a role
•	Have at least one responsibility
•	Or they cannot be active
This stops ghost staff.
________________________________________
2️⃣ Multiple Roles Are Allowed
One person = many roles
But only one active role at a time
This keeps power clean and controlled.
________________________________________
3️⃣ Custom Roles Per School
Each school can create roles like:
•	Exam Officer
•	ICT Coordinator
•	Sports Master
These appear on the ID card just like system roles.
________________________________________
4️⃣ Resigned Staff → Inactive
•	Their data is never deleted
•	History is preserved
•	They cannot log in or act
Used for:
•	Audits
•	Legal records
•	References
________________________________________
5️⃣ Students Leaving → Inactive
•	Removed from:
o	Rankings
o	Reports
o	Analytics
•	Still stored for:
o	Transcripts
o	Verification
________________________________________
6️⃣ Parents Without Active Children → Locked
If all children:
•	Graduate
•	Transfer
•	Withdraw
➡️ Parent role is locked automatically
They cannot access anything until a child is re-linked.
________________________________________
🧠 WHAT THIS LOOKS LIKE IN REAL USE
Example 1: Teacher + Parent
•	Logs in → ID Card opens
•	Sees roles:
o	Teacher
o	Parent
•	Switches role
•	Dashboard changes:
o	Teacher view → lesson plans
o	Parent view → child progress
________________________________________
Example 2: Owner With Multiple Schools
•	Front of card shows:
o	Name
o	3 schools
•	Back shows:
o	Owner
o	Accountant
•	Switch role → different dashboards per school
________________________________________
Example 3: Security Protection
•	Someone hacks a password
•	They still:
o	Can’t access other roles
o	Can’t escalate privileges
o	Can’t guess Ami
________________________________________
🧩 WHY THIS ENGINE IS POWERFUL
✅ Clear identity
✅ Zero role confusion
✅ High security
✅ Scales to many schools
✅ Perfect for audits
✅ Human-friendly
✅ Hacker-resistant
________________________________________
🏁 SIMPLE SUMMARY
The ID Manager is:
•	A digital ID card
•	A role switcher
•	A security gate
•	A responsibility tracker
It ensures:
“Everyone can do only what they are meant to do — nothing more, nothing less.”
________________________________________
3️⃣ DASHBOARDS (ROLE-BASED)
“Everything a student needs — nothing they shouldn’t touch.”
The Student Dashboard is:
•	🎯 Learning-focused
•	🔐 Permission-restricted
•	📊 Analytics-aware
•	💰 Monetization-compatible
•	🤖 AI-enhanced
•	🧱 System-protected
Students interact with content but never control system structure.
________________________________________
📍 SYSTEM POSITIONING
Loads Automatically When:
Active Role = Student
Students:
•	❌ Cannot switch roles
•	❌ Cannot access admin routes
•	❌ Cannot elevate privileges
•	❌ Cannot access other schools
________________________________________
🧭 STRUCTURE (SIDEBAR ARCHITECTURE)
Dashboard
Classroom
   ├── Assignments
   ├── Lesson Notes
   ├── Practice
Exams
Results
Attendance
Library
Tuck Shop
Professor Aura (if enabled)
Messaging
Settings (Limited)
________________________________________
🏠 1. DASHBOARD (HOME)
The dashboard is a summary intelligence screen.
Shows:
•	Upcoming assignment countdown
•	Next scheduled exam (if within 72 hours)
•	Recent scores
•	Attendance percentage
•	Notifications
•	Farming Mode earnings (if enabled)
•	Quick access buttons
Ads:
Visible here if Farming Mode ON.
________________________________________
🏫 2. CLASSROOM TAB
This contains academic learning tools.
________________________________________
📝 ASSIGNMENTS (Inside Classroom)
Students:
Can:
•	View assignment
•	See score
•	See teacher feedback
•	Comment under feedback
•	Upload files
•	Type answers
Cannot:
•	Create assignment
•	Edit instructions
•	Delete submissions
•	See classmates’ work
Status Indicators:
•	Draft
•	Submitted
•	Late
•	Marked
•	Returned for correction
Security:
•	File scanning
•	Timestamp lock
•	Auto-cutoff at deadline
Ads:
❌ Never shown while answering.
________________________________________
📖 LESSON NOTES
Encrypted download system.
Key Feature:
When downloaded:
•	File works ONLY inside Ndovera ecosystem
•	Encrypted format
•	Offline accessible via app
•	Cannot open in external apps
•	Cannot forward or AirDrop
This prevents:
•	Piracy
•	External redistribution
•	Content leaks
Allowed Actions:
•	Read
•	Highlight (local only)
•	Bookmark
•	Offline mode
Ads:
Shown only while browsing, not reading in focus mode.
________________________________________
🧠 PRACTICE (New Structured Feature)
Separate from assignments.
Includes:
•	Auto-generated quizzes
•	Past question practice
•	Weak-area drills
•	AI-generated exercises (if allowed)
Farming Mode:
Ads allowed here.
Rewards enabled.
________________________________________
🧪 3. EXAMS (High Security Zone)
Separate tab.
Not the same as Classroom.
Populated ONLY:
•	On exam day
•	At scheduled time
•	Within approved IP/device window (if configured)
________________________________________
Security Level: MAXIMUM
Features:
•	Full-screen lock (where supported)
•	Tab-switch detection
•	Screenshot detection (where supported)
•	Copy/paste disabled
•	Right-click disabled
•	Auto-submit on:
o	Timeout
o	Disconnection threshold
o	Suspicious activity (if policy enabled)
________________________________________
Supported Question Types:
•	Multiple Choice
•	True/False
•	Matching
•	Short Answer
•	Essay
________________________________________
After Exam:
•	Instant result (objective only) OR
•	Awaiting teacher release
________________________________________
Absolutely Forbidden:
❌ Preview before time
❌ Retake unless authorized
❌ Question download
❌ AI assistance
________________________________________
📊 4. RESULTS
Read-only academic analytics.
Displays:
•	Assignment scores
•	Exam scores
•	Continuous assessment
•	Term result
•	Cumulative progression graph
No:
❌ Ranking comparison
❌ Editing
❌ Hiding
Only active students are included in school analytics.
If status → Inactive:
•	Removed from live metrics
•	Data archived
________________________________________
🕒 5. ATTENDANCE (Read Only)
Shows:
•	Daily attendance
•	Late markers
•	Absence reasons (if recorded)
•	Term attendance %
Students cannot:
•	Modify
•	Appeal directly
•	Delete
Appeals go through Messaging.
________________________________________
📚 6. LIBRARY
Two layers:
________________________________________
A) School Library (Free)
Includes:
•	Textbooks
•	Past questions
•	Recommended materials
•	Borrow status (physical)
________________________________________
B) Ndovera Global Library (Premium Access)
Unlocked using Auras.
Auras:
•	System digital credit
•	Pricing set by Ami
•	Can be purchased or earned
Global Library Includes:
•	International materials
•	Advanced study guides
•	Specialized exam prep
Downloads are encrypted like Lesson Notes.
________________________________________
🛒 7. TUCK SHOP
Full transaction history.
Displays:
•	Item name
•	Quantity
•	Date
•	Amount
•	Payment method
Students cannot:
•	Edit
•	Delete
•	Refund
Parents see same log in Parent Dashboard.
________________________________________
🤖 PROFESSOR AURA (Premium AI System)
AI-powered learning companion.
________________________________________
Capabilities:
✔ Explains concepts step-by-step
✔ Simplifies difficult topics
✔ Generates practice questions
✔ Explains wrong answers
✔ Adjusts difficulty level
✔ Multilingual support (future-ready)
________________________________________
Restrictions:
❌ Cannot write assignments
❌ Cannot answer live exams
❌ Cannot bypass learning
❌ Cannot override teacher authority
________________________________________
AI Modes:
•	Explain Mode
•	Practice Mode
•	Weak Area Mode
•	Exam Review Mode
Usage limits configurable by school.
________________________________________
💬 MESSAGING SYSTEM
Structured and logged.
________________________________________
Students Can Message:
•	Subject teachers
•	Class teacher
•	Admin support
•	Other students (ONLY if school enables peer chat)
________________________________________
Security:
•	Message logging
•	AI moderation
•	Keyword abuse detection
•	Report button
•	Escalation to leadership
No disappearing messages.
No secret chat.
________________________________________
🌱 FARMING MODE (Ad-Integrated Learning Economy)
Optional.
School-controlled.
________________________________________
When ON:
Ads appear in:
•	Dashboard
•	Library browsing
•	Practice
•	Professor Aura
•	Non-exam pages
Never during:
❌ Assignments
❌ Classwork submission
❌ Exams
________________________________________
Rewards System:
Students earn:
•	Coins
•	Badges
•	Points
•	Auras (optional conversion model)
These:
•	Unlock themes
•	Unlock Global Library
•	Unlock AI minutes
•	Unlock avatars
Students cannot toggle ads themselves.
________________________________________
🔐 SYSTEM PROTECTION SUMMARY
Students:
•	Cannot see others’ records
•	Cannot alter system data
•	Cannot escalate role
•	Cannot duplicate content
•	Cannot bypass exam controls
If student leaves:
•	Status → Inactive
•	Removed from rankings
•	Preserved in records
•	Library access revoked
•	Messaging disabled
________________________________________
🧠 TRUE DESIGN PHILOSOPHY
The Ndovera Student Dashboard is:
A Learning Operating System, not a social app.
It balances:
•	Discipline
•	Intelligence
•	Security
•	AI power
•	Monetization
•	Offline usability
•	Data integrity
________________________________________
🏁 FINAL SUMMARY
The student:
✔ Learns
✔ Practices
✔ Submits
✔ Tracks progress
✔ Uses AI responsibly
✔ Earns rewards
✔ Accesses secure content
But:
❌ Never controls structure
❌ Never alters system authority
❌ Never breaks data walls
________________________________________
👨‍👩‍👧 Parent Dashboard
“Visibility, support, and accountability — without academic interference.”
The Parent Dashboard is a monitoring, support, financial, and communication environment.
Parents:
✔ Observe
✔ Support
✔ Pay
✔ Communicate
They do NOT:
❌ Teach
❌ Grade
❌ Examine
❌ Modify academic records
________________________________________
📍 SYSTEM POSITION
Loads Automatically When:
Active Role = Parent
If parent is also:
•	Teacher
•	Staff
•	HoS
•	Owner
Role switching happens via Smart ID Card.
Dashboards remain completely separated.

🔁 CHILDREN SWITCHER (CORE ENGINE)
Location:
Top of dashboard (carousel or dropdown)
Shows per child:
•	Name
•	Photo
•	School
•	Class & Arm
•	Status (Active / Inactive)
Supports:
✔ Multiple children
✔ Multiple schools
✔ Different school sections
✔ Parent also being staff (via role switch)
Rules:
•	Only one child active at a time
•	Switching child refreshes entire dashboard instantly
•	Inactive child:
o	View-only records
o	No live analytics
o	No new messages
If no active children:
•	Parent role becomes Locked (read-only archive access)

Performance Trend Snapshot:
Mini graph across terms or sessions.
________________________________________
🔒 Fee Gating Logic
If Fees == Paid:
✔ Show result
If Fees == Unpaid:
🔒 Lock result
•	Show outstanding balance
•	Show Pay Now button
Once HoS marks Paid:
•	Result unlocks instantly
•	Receipt auto-issued
•	Notification sent
________________________________________
Historical Policy:
✔ All past results remain visible
✔ Archived permanently
✔ Cannot be deleted by parent
✔ Marked “Archived” if student inactive
Newest results always appear on top.

🔐 HARD PERMISSION WALLS
Parents can NEVER:
❌ Write exams
❌ Enter scores
❌ Modify attendance
❌ Grade assignments
❌ Override teachers
❌ Bypass fee gate
❌ Access other students’ data
❌ Escalate privileges
❌ Cash out Auras
________________________________________
🔄 EDGE CASE RULES
If child becomes inactive:
•	Live analytics stop
•	Messaging disabled
•	Results remain archived
•	Library access limited
If parent has no active children:
•	Parent dashboard locks
•	Archive access only
________________________________________
🧠 SYSTEM PHILOSOPHY
The Parent Dashboard is a glass wall.
Parents:
✔ See clearly
✔ Support responsibly
✔ Pay transparently
✔ Communicate safely
But they never:
❌ Distort academics
❌ Manipulate truth
❌ Break system integrity

🕒 1️⃣ CLASS ATTENDANCE
Engine: Teachers tick Present / Absent / Late / Excused.
Features:
•	Daily attendance record
•	Summary dashboard (percent present, absent, late)
•	Bulk entry
•	Attendance reports exportable as PDF/CSV
•	Integration with Student & Parent Dashboards
•	Offline sync
•	Highlight at-risk students
•	Optional alerts if a student misses multiple classes
Rules:
•	Cannot alter archived attendance
•	Audit logs for accountability
•	Class Teacher can review & override
________________________________________
🧮 2️⃣ SUBJECT CA SCORE ENTRY
Features:
•	Enter Continuous Assessment (CA) scores per student
•	Assign weight to CA components (homework, quizzes, projects)
•	Live term total calculation
•	Color-coded highlights for missing scores
•	Bulk entry via spreadsheet upload (offline CSV/Excel)
•	Auto-save drafts with version history
Rules:
•	Only assigned teachers can enter scores (except Class Teacher override)
•	Cannot edit finalized scores unless Class Teacher allows

•	Download pre-formatted spreadsheet
•	Enter offline
•	Upload → auto-validated with logs
•	Works in low connectivity areas

📖 4️⃣ LESSON NOTES
1️⃣ Core Purpose
•	Allow teachers to create, upload, and share lesson notes efficiently.
•	Track engagement and usage for students and parents.
•	Integrate seamlessly with Classroom Tab, AI Tutor, Auras economy, and Analytics.
•	Maintain version history and secure access.
________________________________________
2️⃣ Lesson Note Creation / Upload
Supported Formats:
Type	Examples
Text	.docx, .txt, .md
PDF	.pdf
Slides	.pptx, .key
Images	.jpg, .png, .svg
Audio	.mp3, .wav
Video	.mp4, .mov
Upload Methods:
•	Drag & drop or select files
•	WYSIWYG editor for direct text creation
•	Bulk upload for multiple files per topic/week
________________________________________
3️⃣ Assignment per Subject / Topic / Week
•	Assign lesson notes based on:
o	Subject
o	Topic
o	Week / Academic Period
•	Integration with Student Dashboard Classroom Tab:
o	Students see notes per class automatically
o	AI Tutor can recommend relevant notes based on progress
•	Teachers can schedule notes for future release (e.g., Week 3 notes visible from Monday 8AM)
________________________________________
4️⃣ Visibility & Access Control
Visibility	Who Can See	Notes
Student-only	Students enrolled in class	Parents cannot see
Student + Parent	Students & linked parents	Parents can download/track
Teacher-only	Staff only	Internal resources or reference materials
•	Visibility enforced via RBAC and encrypted access tokens
•	Notes URLs are non-guessable (UUID + token) for security
________________________________________
5️⃣ Tracking Engagement
•	Track Downloads: Count every time a file is downloaded
•	Track Views: Increment view counter each time note is opened (PDF viewer, slides, or text)
•	Engagement Analytics:
o	Which notes are most accessed
o	Student-specific access stats
o	Optional Auras rewards for completing notes reading
•	Logs stored in immutable database table (LessonNoteAnalytics) for compliance
________________________________________
6️⃣ Version History
•	Every update or upload creates a new version automatically
•	Teachers can:
o	Compare versions (side-by-side diff for text or slides)
o	Restore previous versions
•	Metadata includes:
o	Version number
o	Author / uploader
o	Upload timestamp
o	Change notes / comments
•	Immutable archive ensures audit compliance
________________________________________
7️⃣ Advanced Features / Enhancements
Feature	Description
AI Summary	Automatic summary of uploaded notes for students
Note Recommendations	AI Tutor suggests related notes based on student progress
Inline Annotations	Teachers can highlight PDFs or slides directly
Offline Access	Students can download notes for offline reading
Auras Integration	Students earn Auras for completing reading or quizzes on note content
Bulk Assign	Assign multiple notes at once to multiple classes or weeks
________________________________________
8️⃣ UI Flow (Student Perspective)
1.	Go to Classroom Tab → Notes
2.	See list of subjects / topics / weeks
3.	Filter by:
o	Subject
o	Week
o	Type (PDF, slides, video, audio)
4.	Open note → AI Tutor optionally shows summary
5.	Download / mark as read
6.	Auras points awarded automatically if enabled
________________________________________
9️⃣ UI Flow (Teacher / Staff Perspective)
1.	Go to Lesson Notes → Upload / Create
2.	Fill metadata:
o	Subject / Topic / Week
o	Visibility
o	Assign students or parent access
3.	Upload files or create text notes
4.	Publish immediately or schedule release
5.	Track analytics in Dashboard Overview
6.	Access version history to restore old versions if needed
________________________________________
10️⃣ Backend / Database Design
Tables / Codenames for Security / Obfuscation
Table	Codename	Description
lesson_notes	Codex	Stores note metadata (title, subject, topic, week, visibility)
lesson_files	Scrolls	Actual uploaded files (PDFs, slides, videos, audio)
lesson_versions	Chronicles	Version history of notes
lesson_analytics	Spectrometer	Tracks views, downloads, engagement stats
auras_rewards	AuricLedger	Stores points for completed reading
•	Files stored in encrypted cloud storage or CDN with access tokens
•	Metadata and analytics stored in PostgreSQL / encrypted tables
•	Immutable logs for audit compliance
________________________________________
11️⃣ Security Measures
•	RBAC ensures only authorized users see notes
•	Notes URLs are hashed + expiring tokens to prevent direct linking
•	Downloads & views are logged
•	AI summary / recommendations do not expose other student data
•	Offline downloads logged for Auras reward, but file itself is DRM-protected if needed
________________________________________
12️⃣ Integration With NDOVERA Ecosystem
Integration	Notes
Classroom Tab	Notes appear per class / week / subject
AI Tutor	Can read notes, summarize, and generate practice quizzes
Auras Economy	Reward students for completing reading or watching video lessons
Analytics	Spectrometer shows engagement across classes / students / subjects
Live Classes	Notes linked to live class sessions for pre/post-class reading
________________________________________
✅ Outcome
•	Fully featured, secure, and gamified lesson note system
•	Version-controlled and auditable
•	Supports multiple file formats
•	Visibility is finely controlled (Student / Parent / Teacher)
•	Integrated with Classroom, AI Tutor, Auras, and analytics

🗂 5️⃣ LESSON PLAN (Coming Soon)
1️⃣ Purpose
•	Allow teachers to create, schedule, and deliver lesson plans per subject, topic, and week.
•	Integrate with Classroom Tab (enhanced Google Classroom) and Live Classes.
•	Support multi-format lesson materials (text, PDF, slides, images, audio/video).
•	Enable tracking, analytics, and gamification via Auras economy.
•	Maintain secure, version-controlled, and auditable records.
________________________________________
2️⃣ Core Features
a) Lesson Plan Creation
•	Teachers can create lesson plans in rich text or upload:
o	PDF, Slides (PPTX), Images, Audio, Video
•	Assign per:
o	Subject
o	Topic
o	Week / Academic Period
•	Optional pre-defined template layouts (from PortalForge / Blueprint)
•	Optional AI recommendations for related content or practice quizzes
________________________________________
b) Scheduling & Visibility
•	Release scheduling: Lesson plan visible immediately or at a specific date/time
•	Visibility options:
o	Student-only
o	Student + Parent
o	Teacher-only
•	Integrated with Live Class: Lesson plan can be attached to a scheduled live class (pre/post-class materials)
________________________________________
c) Lesson Plan Structure
Each plan includes:
1.	Objectives / Learning Outcomes
2.	Materials / Resources (PDF, slides, media links)
3.	Activities (class exercises, homework, projects)
4.	Assessment (questions, quizzes, or AI-generated exercises)
5.	Notes / Teacher Comments
6.	Auras Rewards (students earn points for completion or engagement)
________________________________________
d) AI Integration
•	AI Tutor: Suggests content, summarizes lesson notes, generates practice questions
•	School Health Advisor: Flags students falling behind or missing live sessions
•	AI Grading / Suggestions: Recommend improvements for teacher lesson plans
________________________________________
e) Tracking & Analytics
•	Views / Engagement: Track student interactions per lesson plan
•	Downloads: Track material downloads
•	Completion: Track which students completed activities or quizzes
•	Auras Ledger: Points awarded automatically for engagement
•	Version History: All lesson plans are version-controlled (teacher can restore older versions)
________________________________________
f) Live Class Integration
•	Each lesson plan can link to live classes:
o	Countdown timer & “Join Live Class” button
o	Automatic attendance tracking
o	Live chat with moderation
o	Recording stored for 1 week
o	AI Tutor can provide real-time summaries or suggestions
________________________________________
g) Multi-Format Support
Format	Description
Text	Rich text notes, HTML/Markdown
PDF	Lecture slides or assignments
Slides	PowerPoint / Keynote / Google Slides exports
Images	Diagrams, charts, illustrations
Audio	Recorded lectures or narrations
Video	Pre-recorded lessons or tutorials
________________________________________
h) Version History & Audit
•	Automatic versioning for each update
•	Metadata stored:
o	Version number
o	Author
o	Upload timestamp
o	Change notes / comments
•	Immutable logs for auditing
________________________________________
i) Gamification & Auras Economy
•	Students earn Auras for:
o	Viewing lesson plans
o	Completing assignments/quizzes
o	Participating in live classes
•	Staff can also earn Auras based on lesson plan activity (monetizable for staff cashout)
•	Rewards and points displayed on Student Dashboard
________________________________________
3️⃣ Dashboard Integration
Student Dashboard
•	Classroom Tab → Lesson Plans
•	Filters by:
o	Subject
o	Week / Topic
o	Material Type (PDF, slides, video, audio)
•	AI Summary pop-up for each lesson
•	“Mark as Completed” button for tracking and Auras points
Teacher Dashboard
•	Create/Upload lesson plans
•	Assign to classes / weeks / topics
•	Schedule release for future visibility
•	Track student engagement and Auras earned
•	Version history & restore functionality
•	Analytics of lesson completion and live class attendance
________________________________________
4️⃣ Backend / Database Design
Tables / Codenames for Security / Obfuscation:
Table	Codename	Purpose
lesson_plans	Codex	Stores lesson plan metadata (title, subject, week, visibility, attached live class)
lesson_materials	Scrolls	Store uploaded files (PDF, slides, images, audio/video)
lesson_versions	Chronicles	Version history of lesson plans
lesson_engagement	Spectrometer	Tracks views, downloads, completion
auras_ledger	AuricRecords	Tracks gamified points earned by students/staff
live_class_links	Oracle	Links between lesson plans and live class sessions
Backend Features:
•	Encrypted storage for files & sensitive data
•	RBAC enforcement (Teacher / Student / Parent / HoS / Super Admin)
•	Audit-logging of every action (upload, delete, edit)
•	Immutable versioning
•	Integration with AI systems (Oracle / AI Tutor)
•	Optional separate Super Admin backend for setting pricing & Auras rewards
________________________________________
5️⃣ Security & Compliance
•	Lesson plan URLs are tokenized → prevents unauthorized access
•	Visibility enforced with role-based access
•	Download logs stored for compliance
•	Immutable audit logs for any edits / deletions
•	Encryption at rest for all uploaded media and PDFs
________________________________________

Lesson Plan → Create / Upload → Assign Subject/Topic/Week → Visibility → Upload Material → AI Recommendations → Schedule Release → Publish

Student Flow:

4️⃣ ATTENDANCE ENGINE (FULL)
👨‍🎓 Student Attendance
STUDENT ATTENDANCE ENGINE — FULL SPEC
Purpose: Track, calculate, and analyze student attendance securely, accurately, and role-controlled, integrating into results, analytics, and parent notifications.
________________________________________
1️⃣ ATTENDANCE DATA STRUCTURE
Field	Description	Notes
StudentID	Unique identifier	FK to Students table
ClassID	Class / Section	FK to Class table
Date	School date	yyyy-mm-dd
MorningStatus	Present / Absent / Late / Excused	Default = Not marked
AfternoonStatus	Present / Absent / Late / Excused	Default = Not marked
MarkedBy	UserID of staff marking	Required
Role	Role of marker	ClassTeacher / Assistant / HoS / Owner / TempStaff
Timestamp	When marked	Auto-generated
Notes	Optional remarks	E.g., Excused sick leave
ApprovalStatus	Approved / Pending / Overridden	Defaults to Approved if Class Teacher or above
________________________________________
2️⃣ ROLE-BASED PERMISSIONS
Role	Can Mark?	Can Override?	Notes
Class Teacher	✅	✅	Full marking for assigned class
Assistant Class Teacher	✅	⚠️ Only delegated	Cannot override Class Teacher unless assigned
HoS	✅	✅	Can mark or override any class
Owner	✅	✅	Full override for emergency/admin
Temporarily Assigned Staff	✅	⚠️ Only delegated	Limited to assigned class & date range
Regular Teacher	❌	❌	Cannot mark unless role elevated
Unauthorized attempts are blocked and logged.
________________________________________
3️⃣ MARKING ENGINE — DAILY FLOW
	Login → Role Validation
	Only users with allowed roles see the Attendance tab.
	Select Class & Date
	Defaults to current date.
	Dropdown for class / section selection if multiple classes assigned.
	Mark Morning & Afternoon Sessions
	Status options:
	Present (P)
	Absent (A)
	Late (L)
	Excused (E) → counts as present in analytics
	Save / Submit
	System validates role + class assignment.
	Attendance saved with timestamp and marker ID.
	Override
	Class Teacher / HoS / Owner can adjust entries.
	System logs original status, new status, marker, timestamp, and reason.
________________________________________
4️⃣ OFFLINE SUPPORT
	Teacher downloads CSV / JSON template for offline marking.
	Template includes: StudentID, MorningStatus, AfternoonStatus, ClassID, Marker Role.
	Fill statuses offline.
	Upload back to system.
	Validation Engine:
	Checks StudentID exists
	Checks Marker Role matches allowed roles
	Checks Date within school calendar
	Conflicts flagged for review:
	Duplicate entries
	Unauthorized upload
	Missing fields
________________________________________
5️⃣ ATTENDANCE CALCULATION ENGINE
Numeric conversion for analytics & results:
Status	Value
Present (P)	1
Late (L)	0.5
Absent (A)	0
Excused (E)	1
Daily Attendance Points = MorningValue + AfternoonValue
Term Attendance % Calculation:
"Attendance %"=(∑("Daily Points" ))/(2×"Total School Days" )×100

Example:
	20 school days → 40 sessions (Morning + Afternoon)
	Student attendance record:
	Present: 30 sessions → 30 points
	Late: 5 sessions → 2.5 points
	Absent: 5 sessions → 0 points
	Attendance % = (30 + 2.5)/40 × 100 = 81.25%
Integration:
	Attendance % feeds into:
	Term results (affective / psychomotor domains)
	AI analytics
	Parent Dashboard
	Reports for HoS / Owner
________________________________________
6️⃣ INTEGRATION WITH RESULTS & ANALYTICS
	Only approved entries (Class Teacher or above) are considered.
	Highlights students below threshold (e.g., <75% attendance).
	Generates alerts for:
	Low attendance
	Repeated lateness
	Patterns across term
	Data used by AI for predictive analysis:
	Risk of underperformance
	Intervention recommendations
________________________________________
7️⃣ PARENT DASHBOARD INTEGRATION
	Parents see:
	Daily attendance (Morning & Afternoon)
	Attendance % per term
	Alerts for absences / lateness
	Inactive students:
	Records read-only
	No live notifications
________________________________________
8️⃣ AUDIT & LOGGING
	Every attendance action logged:
	StudentID, ClassID, Date, Status, MarkerID, MarkerRole, Timestamp, ActionType (Mark/Override)
	Overrides flagged and require reason.
	Supports audit reports for HoS / Owner / Administrator.
________________________________________
9️⃣ ALERTS & NOTIFICATIONS
	Auto-alerts sent to:
	Parents: Daily absent / late
	Class Teacher: Unmarked students
	HoS / Owner: Low attendance trends or mass absenteeism
________________________________________
🔟 SPECIAL RULES
	Inactive students: Attendance not counted for analytics.
	Excused absences: Counts as present (optional configuration).
	Attendance is never editable by students or parents.
	Temporary staff assignments automatically expire.
________________________________________

Teacher / Assistant / HoS / Owner / TempStaff
          │
          ▼
  Attendance Tab (Online/Offline)
          │
          ▼
Role Check → Permission Validation
          │
          ▼
Mark Morning & Afternoon
          │
          ▼
Save → Audit Log Created
          │
          ▼
Class Teacher / HoS / Owner Override (if needed)
          │
          ▼
Calculate Daily Points → Term % → Feeds into:
          ├─ Student Results
          ├─ Parent Dashboard
          ├─ AI Analytics
          ├─ Reports & Alerts
________________________________________
This engine supports:
	Role-controlled marking
	Offline/online marking
	Audit logs
	Integration with results and analytics
	Parent notifications
	Attendance calculation per session & term
👩‍🏫 Staff Attendance
Purpose: Track staff presence accurately, securely, and flexibly, supporting multiple marking methods, offline workflows, and integration with PTA and analytics.
________________________________________
1️⃣ ATTENDANCE METHODS
Staff can mark attendance via three methods:
Method	Details	Notes
Facial Recognition	Staff face scanned and verified	Works on mobile, tablet, or security device
Staff QR Code	Unique QR per staff	Different from PTA QR; scan to mark present
Device-Based	Use own device, another staff device, or security/admin device	Device logs user ID + timestamp
Offline Support:
	All methods support offline queueing.
	Upload/sync occurs when device is online.
	Conflicts auto-flagged for admin review.
________________________________________
2️⃣ ATTENDANCE DATA STRUCTURE
Field	Description	Notes
StaffID	Unique staff identifier	FK to Staff table
Date	yyyy-mm-dd	School calendar date
TimeIn	Clock-in time	Auto timestamp
TimeOut	Clock-out time	Optional, end of day
Method	Facial / QR / Device	Stores attendance type
DeviceID	Device used to mark	Optional
Status	Present / Absent / Late / Excused	Excused optional
MarkedBy	StaffID marking (for device scans)	For shared devices
Notes	Optional remarks	e.g., On-site, Remote, Emergency
PTAFlag	✅ if staff has children and scanned PTA QR	Auto-generated
________________________________________
3️⃣ ROLE-BASED MARKING RULES
Role	Can Mark Attendance	Notes
Staff (any)	✅ Can mark own attendance	Face or QR only
Admin / Security	✅ Can mark any staff	Device or manual override
HoS / Owner	✅ Can override / audit	Emergency / correction only
Temporary Staff / Visitor	✅ Only if assigned	Logged separately
Important:
	Staff cannot mark another staff without device / admin permission.
	Unauthorized attempts are logged and flagged.
________________________________________
4️⃣ PTA INTEGRATION
	Staff with linked children automatically appear in PTA attendance if:
	PTA QR scanned at school events
	Auto-notification to system for parent-child link verification
________________________________________
5️⃣ OFFLINE SUPPORT & SYNC
	Queue attendance locally if internet unavailable.
	Upon reconnect:
	System validates StaffID, DeviceID, Role
	Syncs timestamp and method
	Conflicts flagged for HoS / Admin review
________________________________________
6️⃣ ATTENDANCE CALCULATION & ANALYTICS
Daily / Term calculations:
Status	Value
Present	1
Late	0.5
Absent	0
Excused	1
Metrics:
	Daily % present per department / role

👨‍👩‍👧 PTA Attendance
	👨‍👩‍👧 PTA ATTENDANCE ENGINE
	Purpose:
Track parent participation in school meetings/events. Keeps attendance secure, auditable, and linked to children. Printable reports allow administrative oversight.
	________________________________________
	1️⃣ ATTENDANCE METHOD
	QR-Based:
	Each PTA meeting generates a unique QR code per session
	Parents scan QR on arrival
	QR logs:
	Parent ID
	Meeting ID / Event ID
	Timestamp
	Works on mobile devices (parent app) or school tablets/scanners
	Optional offline scan: queued and synced when online
	Rules:
	One scan per parent per meeting
	Multiple children handled automatically (parent linked to children)
	Invalid QR → rejected, logged
	________________________________________
	2️⃣ ATTENDANCE DATA STRUCTURE
	Field		Description		Notes
	ParentID		Unique parent identifier		FK to Users table
	ChildrenIDs		Linked child(ren)		Auto-filled from student records
	MeetingID		PTA meeting / event identifier		Unique per meeting
	Timestamp		Scan time		Auto-generated
	DeviceID		Device used		Optional for audit
	Status		Present / Absent		Default = Absent; updated after scan
	Notes		Optional		E.g., Late arrival
	________________________________________

	Conflicts flagged for review

Rules: 🧮 CONTINUOUS ASSESSMENT (CA) SCORE SHEET
Purpose:
Track student CA scores per subject, per term, with multi-level review and approval. Fully integrated with attendance, analytics, and results release.
________________________________________
1️⃣ CA SCORE SHEET STRUCTURE
Field	Description	Notes
StudentID	Unique student identifier	FK to Student table
StudentName	Name of student	For display
Class	Class / Section	Auto-filled
Subject	Subject name	Assigned teacher
Term	Term (1/2/3)	Auto-filled
Session	Academic session	Auto-filled
CA Component	e.g., Homework, Classwork, Quiz	Configurable per school
Max Score	Maximum mark for component	e.g., Homework 10, Quiz 20
Score	Score obtained	Entered by Subject Teacher
Total CA	Sum of all components	Auto-calculated
MarkedBy	Teacher who entered score	Auto-logged
DateEntered	Date of entry	Auto-logged
ClassTeacherOverride	Score after Class Teacher override	Optional
OverrideReason	Reason for override	Mandatory if changed
SectionalHeadComment	Comment or recommendation	Optional
HoSApproval	Approved / Returned	Required for result release
ReleaseStatus	Released / Pending / Locked	Auto-updated
________________________________________
2️⃣ WORKFLOW TABLE — CA ENTRY & APPROVAL
Step	Actor	Action	System Behavior	Notes
1	Subject Teacher	Enter CA scores per student	Save as Pending Review	Validation: max score, required fields
2	Class Teacher	Review scores	Can override individual scores	Must provide reason; logs timestamp & actor
3	Sectional Head	Review class results	Approve or request corrections	Adds comments visible to HoS
4	HoS	Final approval	Approve or return for correction	Only approved results → visible in dashboards
5	System	Publish results	Update student / parent dashboard	Fee-gated if needed; integrated with analytics
________________________________________
3️⃣ CA COMPONENT EXAMPLE

Jane Smith	10	15	14	39	39	Needs improvement on Quiz	Approved
Aliyu Bello	7	12	10	29	32	Adjusted for late submission	Returned
Notes:
•	Total CA auto-calculated
•	Override column shows adjustments made by Class Teacher
•	Sectional Head comments are optional but recommended
•	HoSApproval mandatory for release
________________________________________

NDOVERA RESULT MANAGEMENT SYSTEM (RMS) – COMPLETE DESIGN
Purpose:
A secure, auditable, multi-level system for managing all student results, including cognitive, behavioral, psychomotor performance, attendance, grading, and exam practice, fully integrated with dashboards for students, parents, and staff.
________________________________________
1️⃣ SYSTEM MODULES
Module	Purpose	Key Features
CA Management	Continuous Assessment input and validation	Subject-wise CA entry, offline upload, bulk entry, Class Teacher override, Sectional Head review, HoS approval
Exam Management (Official)	Official exams written via Exam tab	Scores auto-captured into RMS, multi-level approval (Teacher → Class Teacher → Sectional Head → HoS), security features (timer, anti-tab-switch, auto-submit)
CBT Management (Practice)	Exam preparation and practice	Practice exams for Common Entrance, BECE, WAEC, JAMB, SAT, TOEFL, IGCSE etc., AI feedback, does not feed into Result Sheet
Attendance Integration	Daily & term attendance tracked	Morning/Afternoon, Present/Absent/Late, feeds into Result Sheet for cumulative performance
Cognitive Card	Academic summary per subject	CA + Exam → Total, Subject Position, Highest/Lowest marks, Class Average, HoS-approved Grade & Remark, color-coded card
Behavioral / Affective Card	Track personality / behavioral traits	Radio-button input, school-customizable traits, color-coded, Class Teacher ticks, integrated into results
Psychomotor Card	Track practical / physical growth	Beginning/Ending Height & Weight, optional growth trends, editable per term
Grading Scale Management	Define school grading system	Customizable by HoS / Proprietor, grades, remarks, colors, approval required to appear in results
Comments & Signatures	Teacher, Sectional Head, HoS	Optional per student, audit-logged, HoS signature required for official release
Watermark & Branding	Authenticity	Logo watermark, position (center/bottom right/custom), transparency, background image
Audit & Approval Workflow	Multi-level verification	Tracks every entry, edit, override, approval; unapproved results cannot be released
Reports & Analytics	School-wide insights	Class averages, subject trends, at-risk students, AI analytics, export to PDF/CSV
Dashboards	Role-based visibility	Student, Parent, Teacher, HoS, Proprietor; fee-gated access for parents
AI & Premium Features	Optional advanced analytics	Predictive performance insights, intervention suggestions, cognitive trend analysis

CBT
CATION FLOW
STEP 1: NORMALIZATION (Before Any Comparison)
When a question is submitted (typed, pasted, uploaded):
The system normalizes it:
•	Convert to lowercase
•	Remove punctuation
•	Remove extra spaces
•	Standardize symbols (× → *, ÷ → /)
•	Remove numbering (1., (a), Q1)
•	Strip formatting tags
👉 Output: normalized_question_text
________________________________________
STEP 2: HASHING (Fast Exact Match)
Generate hashes:
•	question_hash = SHA-256(normalized_question_text)
•	options_hash = SHA-256(normalized_options_text)
Check database:
•	If question_hash exists → ❌ Duplicate (Block)
•	If not → continue
________________________________________
STEP 3: SEMANTIC SIMILARITY (System, Not AI)
Use:
•	Token overlap
•	N-grams (bi-grams / tri-grams)
•	Subject + topic + exam type matching
Score similarity:
•	90–100% → ❌ Duplicate (Block)
•	75–89% → ⚠️ Similar (Flag for review)
•	<75% → ✅ Accept as new
⚠️ Similar questions require manual approval before activation.
________________________________________
STEP 4: ANSWER CONSISTENCY CHECK
If a similar question exists:
•	Compare correct answer
•	If answers conflict → Admin review required
•	If answers match → link to existing question
________________________________________
🧠 DEDUPLICATION DECISION TABLE
Condition	Action
Exact hash match	Block
High similarity	Flag
Medium similarity	Review
Low similarity	Accept
Same question, no answer	Trigger AI once
________________________________________
2️⃣ QUESTION BANK DATABASE SCHEMA
(Clean, reusable, audit-safe)
🗄️ questions table
Field	Type	Purpose
id	UUID	Global unique ID
question_text	TEXT	Original text
normalized_text	TEXT	For matching
question_hash	VARCHAR	Deduplication
subject_id	FK	Subject
topic_id	FK	Topic
exam_type	ENUM	CBT / Exam / Assignment
difficulty	ENUM	Easy / Medium / Hard

4️⃣ CBT + EXAM + ASSIGNMENT REUSE MAPPING
(One Question → Many Engines)
________________________________________

It is referenced, not copied.

Engine	Behavior

Online Exam	Timed, strict, auto-score
Offline Exam	Printed, manual score entry
Assignment	Homework / classwork

Engine	Timer	Strict	Result Impact
CBT	Optional	Medium	❌ No

Exam (Offline)	N/A	Physical	✅ Yes
Assignment	Optional	Low	✅ Yes

6️⃣ FEES ENGINE
💰 NDOVERA FINANCE & PAYMENTS MANAGEMENT SYSTEM
“Transparent, controlled, per-child, audit-safe.”
________________________________________
🧠 CORE FINANCIAL PRINCIPLES (NON-NEGOTIABLE)
1.	Fees are per child, not per class
2.	Results are locked if fees are outstanding
3.	HoS / Tenant School Owner controls fees by default
4.	Accountant sees revenue, not fee policy (unless permitted)
5.	Receipts are the ultimate proof of payment
6.	Every transaction is auditable and reversible (not deletable)
________________________________________
1️⃣ FEE STRUCTURE MANAGEMENT
🎯 WHO MANAGES FEES?
Role	Capability
HoS	Full fee control
School Owner	Full fee control
Accountant	❌ No fee control (unless explicitly permitted)
Ami (Super Admin)	Emergency override
________________________________________
🧾 FEE COMPONENTS (PER CHILD)
•	Tuition
•	Extra Care
•	Welfare
•	Custom Items
o	Transport
o	Feeding
o	Books
o	Uniform (optional)
o	Any school-defined item
Each item has:
•	Amount
•	Term applicability
•	Mandatory / optional flag
________________________________________
🧮 CALCULATION ENGINE
Total Expected =
Tuition + Extra Care + Welfare + Custom Items

Final Payable =
Total Expected - Scholarships - Discounts
Recalculates automatically when:
•	A badge is applied
•	A payment is recorded
•	A fee item is modified
________________________________________
2️⃣ BADGES & AUTOMATIC DISCOUNTS
🏷 BADGE TYPES
🎓 Scholarship Badge
•	100% tuition waiver
•	Partial (percentage or fixed)
•	Item-specific (e.g. tuition only)
👨‍🏫 Staff Child Badge
•	Predefined discount rules
•	Can exclude specific fee items
👨‍👩‍👧 Multi-Child Family Badge
•	Automatically applied when:
o	Parent has ≥2 active children
•	Discount logic:
o	Flat % per additional child
o	Tiered discount (e.g. 5%, 10%, 15%)
🎯 Custom Discount Badge
•	Term-specific or permanent
•	Time-bound
•	Fully auditable
Badges:
•	Apply instantly
•	Cannot be silently removed
•	Require HoS/Owner approval

NDOVERA Receipts – Mock Layout

•	Dynamic Receipt Number: e.g., NDV-RCPT-00001234

•	School Details: Name, Logo, Address
•	Transaction Details: Date, Payment Type, Amount, Auras used (if applicable)
•	Payment Mode: Bank transfer, mobile wallet, card, or cash
•	Transaction ID: For backend tracking and audit
•	QR Code / Verification Code: Optional for authenticity
•	Footer: Notes, Terms, Contact Info

3️⃣ Optional Enhancements
•	Color-coded sections: Payments vs Auras transactions
•	Logo watermark for authenticity

•	Printable & PDF-friendly: Standard A4 layout
•	Multi-language support: English + local language
•	Audit-ready backend logs: Every receipt stored in immutable table
________________________________________
4️⃣ Backend / Data Flow
Tables / Codename:
Table	Codename	Purpose
transactions	AuricExits	Tracks all payments, cashouts, and Auras spending
users	CipherIndex	ID, role, email for receipt generation
schools	ColonyLedger	School details & logos
receipt_logs	SentinelRecords	Immutable log of generated receipts
Flow:
1.	Payment processed → saved in AuricExits
2.	Receipt generated → saved in receipt_logs
3.	PDF/A4 or print-ready version created → available to user
4.	QR/Verification code links back to receipt entry in SentinelRecords
________________________________________
This layout can handle all NDOVERA transactions, including:
•	Student fees
•	Parent Auras top-ups
•	Staff cashout
•	Donations & merch purchases

📚 NDOVERA LIBRARY SYSTEM
(Physical + Digital • Paid + Free • AI-Assisted • Revenue-Sharing)
________________________________________
1️⃣ LIBRARY MODES
NDOVERA Library operates in 4 integrated modes:
A. 📖 Physical Library (School-Owned)
•	Traditional borrowing
•	Offline borrowing allowed
•	Librarian confirms returns
B. 📱 Digital Reading (NDOVERA Books)
•	Read inside app (no download)
•	Paid or free (₦0 / 0 Auras allowed)
C. 🧑‍💻 User-Submitted Digital Library
•	Users upload books
•	Other users read for a fee
•	Revenue split applies
D. 🏫 Multi-School Shared Library
•	All tenant schools share:
o	Question banks
o	Books
o	Academic materials
•	Permissions controlled per school
________________________________________
2️⃣ USER ROLES & VISIBILITY
Who Can See What?
Role	Access
Student	Read, borrow, history, UPLOAD BOOKS
Parent	VIEW CHILD’S HISTORY, Read, borrow, history, UPLOAD BOOKS
Librarian	Manage borrow/return, READ, UPLOAD AND HISTORY
Teacher	Recommend books, Read, borrow, UPLOAD BOOKS
Contributor	Upload & earnings
NDOVERA Admin	Review & approve

9️⃣ FARMING MODE (EDUCATORS APPRECIATION)
Purpose: Generate monetization without disrupting learning while incentivizing engagement.
________________________________________
1️⃣ Farming Mode Basics
•	Optional Activation: Users can enable/disable Farming Mode at will.
•	Ads Integration:
o	Slightly shrinks content area.
o	Does not appear during assignments, exams, or assessments.
o	Appears in:
	Lesson notes
	Library browsing
	Dashboard navigation
	AI practice sessions
	CBT (Computer-Based Tests)
•	Auras Earned:
Non-monetary points (configurable by super admin) for:
o	Completing lessons
o	Reading library books
o	Submitting approved assignments
o	Completing practice/CBT exercises
•	Display: Coins, badges, or points visible on the dashboard.
•	Invisible Exchange Rate: Users see only “Auras,” not actual revenue.
________________________________________
2️⃣ Cashout Rules
Role	Cashout Eligible?	Notes
Staff	✅ Yes	After 2 months of accumulation and active Farming Mode for 2 months
Parents	❌ No	Can transfer Auras to children but cannot cash out
Students	❌ No	Can only spend in-app
Accumulation Timeline for Staff:
•	Month 1–2: Collect Auras through engagement.
•	End of Month 2 (18th):
o	Staff become eligible for cashout.
o	System resets the accumulated Auras and activates monthly cashout.
•	Month 3:
o	Must withdraw within 7 days.
o	If unclaimed → balance resets, automatic reminders sent.
________________________________________
3️⃣ Parents & Students Rules
•	Cannot withdraw cash.
•	Can spend Auras on:
o	AI Tutor usage
o	Library reading (NDOVERA & premium books)
o	Optional in-app purchases or educational add-ons
•	Auras reset every 3 months if unused.
o	Accumulation history preserved for analytics.
________________________________________
4️⃣ Backend Mechanics
Table	Description
farming_mode_config	Enabled/disabled per school & role
auras_transactions	Logs every earning & spending action
auras_balance	Current balance per user
auras_reset_schedule	Tracks 3-month reset windows
auras_cashout_log	Staff withdrawals, audit-ready
Audit Rules:
•	No manual balance modification.
•	Logs are immutable for compliance.
•	School Admin / HoS can view reports but cannot alter student/parent balances.
________________________________________
5️⃣ User Experience (UI Flow)
Staff:
1.	Dashboard shows Auras balance.
2.	Click Cashout when eligible.
3.	Enter payment details (bank / mobile wallet).
4.	Transaction confirmed → logged in auras_cashout_log.
Students & Parents:
1.	Dashboard shows Auras balance.
2.	Spend on allowed features:
o	AI Tutor
o	Library books
3.	Receive alerts for upcoming reset.
________________________________________
6️⃣ Notifications & Reminders
Staff:
•	Month 2: “You are now eligible to cash out.”
•	7-day countdown reminder before reset.
Parents / Students:
•	Pre-reset reminder: “Unused Auras will expire in X days.”
________________________________________
7️⃣ Analytics
Accessible to School Admin / Owner / HoS:
•	Total Auras earned per role
•	Auras spent per category

1️⃣3️⃣ SECURITY & GOVERNANCE
🔐 NDOVERA ROBUST SECURITY FRAMEWORK
Ndovera is built on four non-negotiable pillars:
1️⃣ Strict Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)
2️⃣ Hard Tenant Data Isolation
3️⃣ Immutable Audit Logging
4️⃣ Zero Personal Visibility for Super Admin
________________________________________
1️⃣ STRICT RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)
Every action is permission-based.
Roles Include:
•	Super Admin (Platform level only)
•	School Owner
•	HoS
•	Principal
•	Head Teacher
•	Teacher
•	ICT Officer
•	Parent
•	Student
Enforcement Layers:
Layer	Protection
UI Guard	Buttons hidden if unauthorized
API Guard	Backend blocks illegal requests
Database Guard	Queries always filtered by school_id
No role inherits permissions automatically.
No hidden privileges.
________________________________________
2️⃣ HARD TENANT DATA ISOLATION
Each school operates in a sealed data boundary.
Isolation Rules:
•	Every record tagged with school_id
•	All queries scoped by tenant
•	Media stored per-school directory
•	Cross-school joins blocked
Even if two schools:
•	Use same template
•	Have same student names
•	Operate in same city
Their data never touches.
________________________________________
3️⃣ IMMUTABLE AUDIT LOGS
Every sensitive action is logged:
•	Account creation
•	Role change
•	Data edits
•	Auras spending
•	Cashout
•	AI usage
•	Website deployment
•	Login printing
Logs are:
•	Append-only
•	Timestamped
•	Non-editable
•	Visible to authorized governance roles only
Even Super Admin cannot delete logs.
________________________________________
4️⃣ SUPER ADMIN PRIVACY RESTRICTIONS
Super Admin can:
•	Enable/suspend schools
•	View aggregated platform statistics
•	Manage templates
•	Configure pricing
Super Admin cannot:
•	View student names
•	View parent contact
•	View student grades
•	View school fee records
•	Access login credentials
•	Impersonate users
Platform-level control ≠ Data access.
________________________________________
🆔 NDOVERA IDENTITY SYSTEM (STANDARDIZED)
All users receive system-generated IDs.
IDs are:
•	Auto-generated
•	Immutable
•	Non-editable
•	Never recycled
•	Unique per school
________________________________________
🎓 STUDENT ID FORMAT
NL-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
Example:
NL-GIS-000145
•	NL = Ndovera Learner
•	Incremental per school
•	Cannot be changed
Email format (masked display):
jo***@schoolname.com
________________________________________
👩‍🏫 STAFF ID FORMAT
NS-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
Example:
NS-GIS-000032
•	NS = Ndovera Staff
________________________________________
👨‍👩‍👧 PARENT ID FORMAT
NP-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
Example:
NP-GIS-000087
•	NP = Ndovera Parent
•	One parent can link to multiple children
________________________________________
GLOBAL ID RULES
•	Generated during onboarding only
•	Linked permanently to tenant
•	Visible in place of sensitive identifiers
•	Used for all reporting & auditing
________________________________________
📧 SYSTEM-MANAGED EMAIL STRUCTURE
Emails are internal system emails.
Format:
username@schoolname.com
Displayed as masked:
jo***@schoolname.com
Rules:
•	Personal emails never exposed
•	Internal routing only
•	Cannot be edited manually
•	Used for platform notifications
________________________________________
🖨 PRINTING LOGIN DETAILS (A4 CONTROLLED DISTRIBUTION)
Allowed for:
✅ HoS
✅ ICT Officer
❌ Teachers
❌ Parents
❌ Students
❌ Super Admin
________________________________________
WHEN CAN LOGIN DETAILS BE PRINTED?
Only during onboarding phase.
Only for users who:
•	Have never logged in
•	Still have temporary password active
________________________________________
WHAT IS PRINTED?
Column	Value
Public ID	NL / NS / NP formatted ID
System Email	school-managed email
Temporary Password	auto-generated
Role	User role
Login URL	Portal address
________________________________________
SECURITY CONTROLS FOR PRINTING
1️⃣ One-Time Visibility
•	Temporary password visible once
•	After first login:
o	Password deleted permanently
o	Cannot be reprinted
________________________________________
2️⃣ Print Token Protection
•	ICT/HoS must confirm action
•	System generates limited-time print token
•	Token expires within minutes
________________________________________
3️⃣ Expiry Enforcement
•	If user does not log in within X days:
o	Temporary password expires
o	Reset required
________________________________________
4️⃣ Audit Logging
Each print action logs:
•	Who printed
•	Role
•	School ID
•	Number of credentials printed
•	Timestamp
•	Device/IP (optional)
Immutable.
________________________________________
A4 PRINT FORMAT (Professional & Secure)
Header:
SCHOOL NAME
NDOVERA LOGIN DETAILS
Session / Term
Table:
ID | Email | Temp Password | Role
Footer:
Login URL
⚠️ Change password immediately after first login
Optional:
•	Watermark
•	Page numbering
•	Distribution tracking ID
________________________________________
🚫 PROHIBITED ACTIONS
•	No password reprint after first login
•	No exporting credentials to Excel
•	No emailing plain passwords
•	No Super Admin access to credentials
•	No bypass of print logs
________________________________________
🔐 FINAL SECURITY OUTCOME
✔ Strict permission enforcement
✔ Full tenant isolation
✔ Secure identity standardization
✔ Controlled onboarding credential printing
✔ Immutable audit logs
✔ Super Admin cannot spy on schools
✔ Legally defensible architecture
________________________________________
This now forms the core trust foundation of Ndovera.

SUPER ADMIN(AMI)
Ndovera SuperAdmin (Ami) – Full Design Blueprint
1️⃣ Core Philosophy
•	Ami is a modular fortress inside NDOVERA.
•	Operates independently with its own backend (codename: “Vault”).
•	Frontend is lazy-loaded inside main NDOVERA app only for Super Admins.
•	Security-by-design with unconventional terms to make automated scraping or brute-force more difficult.
________________________________________
2️⃣ Access & Authentication
•	Codename: Gatekeeper handles all login sessions.
•	Uses JWT with HMAC + refresh tokens.
•	Multi-factor authentication mandatory for super admins.
•	Role-based access enforced:
o	AmiMaster = full system
o	AmiObserver = read-only analytics
o	AmiOperator = can modify templates & pricing, not delete schools
•	Tokens encrypted with AES-256 before storing in local storage.
________________________________________
3️⃣ Frontend Structure (React / TSX Modular)
Lazy-loaded modules (loaded only if role=SuperAdmin):
Module	Codename	Function
Tenant Management	Colony	Add/remove schools, onboard HoS, define school initials
Template Control	Blueprint	Add/remove templates, assign template to school, manage pages
Pricing & Auras	AuricVault	Set price in Auras for AI Tutor, premium books, optional paid features
Analytics & Metrics	Spectrometer	Aggregate school stats: Auras economy, attendance, academic performance, unclaimed rewards
Audit & Governance	Sentinel	Immutable logs of every action, print login requests, cashout logs
AI Systems	Oracle	Oversee AI Tutor, School Health Advisor, performance predictions across all tenants
Deployment & Website	PortalForge	Activate tenant websites at midnight, manage pages, SEO, responsive layout
User Management	Cipher	Create, manage, mask emails/IDs (NL / NS / NP / NA), print login details securely
Security Settings	Rampart	Configure RBAC, enable/disable farming mode, enforce password policies
Frontend Lazy Loading Example:
const Colony = lazy(() => import("./modules/Colony"));
const Blueprint = lazy(() => import("./modules/Blueprint"));
const AuricVault = lazy(() => import("./modules/AuricVault"));
Note: Each module is self-contained with independent state management (Redux Toolkit or Zustand) and secure API calls.
________________________________________
4️⃣ Backend Design (Vault)
•	Backend stack (robust and impregnable):
o	Node.js / NestJS for modular architecture
o	PostgreSQL with row-level security & encryption-at-rest
o	Redis for caching and session management
o	Nginx as reverse proxy + WAF (Web Application Firewall)
o	Rate-limiting, IP whitelisting, geo-blocking for admin endpoints
•	Tables & Roles (secure / unconventional terms):
Table	Codename	Purpose
schools_registry	ColonyLedger	Tenant school info, HoS IDs, initials
template_inventory	BlueprintArchive	All available templates & page layouts
auras_pricing	AuricRates	Stores prices of AI lessons/books in Auras
audit_logs	SentinelRecords	Immutable append-only audit logs
user_credentials	CipherIndex	IDs, masked emails, temporary passwords
cashout_transactions	AuricExits	Staff Auras withdrawals, automatic reset logic
analytics_aggregate	SpectrometerData	School-level aggregated stats
ai_activity	OracleRecords	AI Tutor usage, Health Advisor insights
Security Features:
•	End-to-end encryption for sensitive data
•	Immutable append-only logs (SentinelRecords)
•	Row-level security ensures Ami cannot see individual student passwords; only masked IDs
•	Rate-limit endpoints to prevent abuse
•	Two separate DBs possible:
o	mainDB for tenant operations
o	vaultDB for super admin operations (never exposed to main users)
________________________________________
5️⃣ Unconventional Terms / Security Through Obscurity
•	Tenant IDs → ColonyID
•	Templates → Blueprints
•	Auras → Aurics
•	Analytics → Spectrometer
•	Audit Logs → Sentinel
•	Cashouts → AuricExit
•	AI Tutor → Oracle
•	Website Builder → PortalForge
•	Passwords → CipherTokens
This obfuscates backend and API endpoints from simple inspection, making scraping and brute-force attacks harder.
________________________________________
6️⃣ Super Admin Features Summary
a) Colony (Tenant Management)
•	Onboard HoS, staff, parents, students
•	Assign school initials, ID generation rules
•	Masked emails & IDs (NL/NS/NP/NA)
•	One-time login printout (A4) with audit logging
b) Blueprint (Template Control)
•	Add/remove up to 10 pages per template
•	Assign templates to schools
•	Responsive & SEO optimized
•	Auto-activation at midnight
c) AuricVault (Pricing & Auras)
•	Set prices for AI Tutor lessons & premium books
•	Optional paid features (merch, donations)
•	Role-based cashout eligibility for staff
•	Invisible exchange rate visible to students/parents
d) Spectrometer (Analytics)
•	Aggregate statistics per school & role
•	Engagement metrics (lessons completed, library reads, CBT attempts)
•	Unclaimed Auras & cashout tracking
•	Export to PDF/Excel with masked IDs
e) Sentinel (Audit & Governance)
•	Logs all actions: onboarding, login printing, cashouts, template edits
•	Immutable & append-only
•	Exportable for compliance
f) Oracle (AI Oversight)
•	AI Tutor usage tracking
•	School Health Advisor insights (attendance vs results, fee default risk, student risk alerts)
•	Teacher AI workload insights
g) PortalForge (Website Deployment)
•	Manage school websites
•	Templates pre-filled for beginners
•	Activate at 12AM automatically
•	Up to 10 pages per school, each with independent layouts
________________________________________
7️⃣ Modular Frontend / Backend Flow
NDOVERA Main App
 ├─ Students/Staff/Parents
 │    └─ Main Backend (mainDB)
 │        ├─ Classes / Lessons / Attendance / Auras / AI
 │        └─ RBAC enforced
 └─ SuperAdmin (Ami Module)
      ├─ Lazy-loaded React module
      └─ Vault Backend (vaultDB)
           ├─ Colony (Tenant mgmt)
           ├─ Blueprint (Templates)
           ├─ AuricVault (Pricing)
           ├─ Sentinel (Audit)
           ├─ Spectrometer (Analytics)
           ├─ Oracle (AI oversight)
           └─ PortalForge (Website deploy)
Integration: Ami APIs are REST or GraphQL endpoints, secured via JWT tokens + AES encryption. Main app can call only permitted endpoints if required.
________________________________________
8️⃣ Security & Impregnability Highlights

💬 NDOVERA MESSAGING & QUESTION BANK SYSTEM
(Communication + Academic Intelligence Layer)
NDOVERA treats communication and questions as core school infrastructure, not add-ons.
________________________________________
PART 1️⃣ — NDOVERA MESSAGING SYSTEM
WhatsApp-Like, but Role-Controlled
________________________________________
🎯 PURPOSE
The NDOVERA Messaging System allows real-time communication between school stakeholders while enforcing strict visibility rules, especially for parents and students.
✔ Familiar WhatsApp-style interface
✔ Real-time chat (online & offline-first)
✔ File sharing, voice notes, images
✔ Read receipts & typing indicators
✔ Role-based contact visibility
✔ School-safe, auditable communication
________________________________________
📱 USER EXPERIENCE (WHAT IT FEELS LIKE)
To the user, it feels like WhatsApp:
Chat list on the left
Active conversation on the right
Message bubbles
Timestamps
Delivered ✓✓ and Read ✓✓✓
“Typing…” indicators
Attachments (PDF, images, audio)
But behind the scenes, NDOVERA controls who can see who.
________________________________________
👥 CONTACT VISIBILITY RULES (VERY IMPORTANT)
👨‍👩‍👧 PARENTS SEE ONLY:
✔ Their children’s teachers
✔ Their children’s class teachers
✔ School administrators
✔ Tuckshop manager
✔ NDOVERA Help Centre
❌ Parents cannot:
See other parents
See unrelated teachers
Message random staff
Message other students
________________________________________
👩‍🏫 TEACHERS SEE:
✔ Students they teach
✔ Parents of those students
✔ Other teachers
✔ School admins
✔ NDOVERA Help Centre
________________________________________
🎓 STUDENTS SEE:
✔ Their subject teachers
✔ Class teacher
✔ School announcements channel
✔ NDOVERA Help Centre
❌ No student-to-student private chat (unless explicitly enabled by school)
________________________________________
🧑‍💼 ADMIN / OWNER / HoS SEE:
✔ Everyone
✔ Broadcast channels
✔ System notifications
________________________________________

1️⃣ One-to-One Chats
Parent ↔ Teacher
Student ↔ Teacher
Staff ↔ Staff
________________________________________

Class group (Class Teacher + Students + Parents)
Subject group (Teacher + Students)
Staff group
Management group
✔ Only admins can create sensitive groups
✔ Group membership auto-updated from class data
________________________________________
3️⃣ Official Channels (Read-Only)
School Announcements
Exam Notices
Fee Notices
NDOVERA Updates

MESSAGING(CHATS)
