import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { UserRole, User, Message, Conversation } from '../../../shared/types/index';
import { Search, Send, Paperclip, ChevronLeft, Plus, CheckCircle2 } from 'lucide-react';

import NewConversationModal from './NewConversationModal';

const ConversationListItem = ({ conversation, isActive, onClick }) => {
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`w-full text-left p-4 border-l-4 ${isActive ? 'border-emerald-500 bg-slate-800/50' : 'border-transparent hover:bg-slate-800/30'}`}>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <img src={conversation.user_avatar} alt={conversation.user_name} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/>
        <div className="flex-1">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
            <p className="font-bold text-sm text-slate-200">{conversation.user_name}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">{new Date(conversation.last_message_timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}</p>
          </div>
          <p className="text-xs text-slate-400 truncate pr-4">{conversation.last_message_text}</p>
        </div>
        {conversation.unread_count > 0 && <div className="w-4 h-4 bg-emerald-500 text-white text-[10px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-full font-bold">{conversation.unread_count}</div>}
      </div>
    </button>
  );
};

const ChatMessage = ({ message, isYou, users, currentUser }) => {
  const sender = users[message.sender_id];
  if (!sender) return null; // Don't render message if sender is not found

  const otherUserIds = Object.keys(users).filter(key => key !== currentUser.id);
  let readByList = [];
  try {
    if (typeof message.read_by === 'string') {
      readByList = JSON.parse(message.read_by);
    } else if (Array.isArray(message.read_by)) {
      readByList = message.read_by;
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Failed to parse read_by:", message.read_by);
  }
  const isRead = readByList.length > 0 && otherUserIds.some(id => readByList.includes(id));

  return (
    <div className={`flex items-end gap-2 ${isYou ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
        {!isYou && <img src={sender.avatarUrl} alt={sender.name} className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/>}
        <div className={`max-w-xs p-3 rounded-2xl ${isYou ? 'bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-br-none' : 'bg-slate-800 text-slate-200 rounded-bl-none'}`}>
            <p className="text-sm">{message.text}</p>
            {message.attachment && (
              <div className="mt-2">
                {message.attachment.file_type.startsWith('image/') ? (
                  <img src={message.attachment.file_path} alt={message.attachment.file_name} className="rounded-lg" />
                ) : (
                  <a href={message.attachment.file_path} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" className="text-emerald-400 underline">{message.attachment.file_name}</a>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1 mt-1">
              <p className={`text-[10px] ${isYou ? 'text-emerald-200' : 'text-slate-500'}`}>{new Date(message.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}</p>
              {isYou && isRead && <CheckCircle2 className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-200" />}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default function MessagingScreen({ onBack }) {
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false);
  const [onlineUsers, setOnlineUsers] = useState(new Set());
  const [conversations, setConversations] = useState([]);
  const [activeConversation, setActiveConversation] = useState(null);
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
  const [users, setUsers] = useState({});
  const [newMessage, setNewMessage] = useState('');
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [searchResults, setSearchResults] = useState([]);
  const ws = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null);

  const currentUser = { id: 'user_teacher_1' }; // This would come from auth in a real app

  useEffect(() => {
    // Fetch initial data
    async function fetchData() {
      try {
        const usersRes = await fetch('/api/users');
        if (!usersRes.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch users');
        const usersData = await usersRes.json();
        const usersMap = usersData.reduce((acc, user) => ({ ...acc, [user.id]: user }), {});
        setUsers(usersMap);

        const convRes = await fetch('/api/conversations');
        if (!convRes.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch conversations');
        const convData = await convRes.json();
        setConversations(convData);
        if (convData.length > 0) {
          setActiveConversation(convData[0]);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching initial data:', error);
      }
    }
    fetchData();

    // WebSocket connection
    const wsUrl = `wss://${window.location.host}`;
    ws.current = new WebSocket(wsUrl);

    ws.current.onmessage = (event) => {
      const received = JSON.parse(event.data);
      if (received.type === 'online_users') {
        setOnlineUsers(new Set(received.users));
      } else if (received.type === 'typing') {
        if (received.conversation_id === activeConversation?.conversation_id) {
          setIsTyping(true);
        }
      } else if (received.type === 'stop_typing') {
        setIsTyping(false);
      } else {
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, received]);
      }
    };

    // ... (WebSocket logic remains the same)

    // Register service worker and subscribe to push notifications
    if ('serviceWorker' in navigator && 'PushManager' in window) {
      navigator.serviceWorker.register('/sw.js')
        .then(swReg => {
          console.log('Service Worker is registered', swReg);

          return swReg.pushManager.getSubscription()
            .then(subscription => {
              if (subscription === null) {
                // Create a new subscription
                const vapidPublicKey = 'BBTmUE1gnNecXMvbuR_8-dTfFi2T6NGERAMhTrcB09YRuFLQYXnWPd3petdB1jDsIQ7eP4a-4BeMRyDHzab5r6I';
                return swReg.pushManager.subscribe({
                  userVisibleOnly: true,
                  applicationServerKey: urlBase64ToUint8Array(vapidPublicKey)
                });
              } else {
                // We have a subscription
                return subscription;
              }
            })
            .then(subscription => {
              // Send the subscription to the server
              fetch('/api/subscribe', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: JSON.stringify({ subscription, userId: currentUser.id }),
                headers: {
                  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                }
              });
            });
        })
        .catch(error => {
          console.error('Service Worker Error', error);
        });
    }

    return () => ws.current?.close();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeConversation) {
      async function fetchMessages() {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/messages/${activeConversation.conversation_id}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        setMessages(data);

        // Mark messages as read
        data.forEach(msg => {
          let readByList = [];
          try {
            if (typeof msg.read_by === 'string') {
              readByList = JSON.parse(msg.read_by);
            } else if (Array.isArray(msg.read_by)) {
              readByList = msg.read_by;
            }
          } catch (e) {
            console.error("Failed to parse read_by:", msg.read_by);
          }

          if (msg.sender_id !== currentUser.id && !readByList.includes(currentUser.id)) {
            ws.current?.send(JSON.stringify({
              type: 'message_read',
              message_id: msg.id,
              user_id: currentUser.id,
            }));
          }
        });
      }
      fetchMessages();
    }
  }, [activeConversation]);

  const handleSendMessage = () => {
    if (newMessage.trim() === '' || !ws.current || !activeConversation) return;

    const message = {
      id: `msg_${Date.now()}`,
      conversation_id: activeConversation.conversation_id,
      sender_id: currentUser.id,
      text: newMessage,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
    };

    ws.current.send(JSON.stringify(message));
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, message]);
    setNewMessage('');
  };

  const handleTyping = (isTyping) => {
    if (!ws.current || !activeConversation) return;
    ws.current.send(JSON.stringify({
      type: isTyping ? 'typing' : 'stop_typing',
      conversation_id: activeConversation.conversation_id,
      user_id: currentUser.id,
    }));
  }

  const handleFileUpload = async (event) => {
    const file = event.target.files[0];
    if (!file || !activeConversation) return;

    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('file', file);

    const res = await fetch('/api/upload', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData,
    });

    const data = await res.json();

    // Create a new message with the attachment
    const message = {
      id: `msg_${Date.now()}`,
      conversation_id: activeConversation.conversation_id,
      sender_id: currentUser.id,
      text: '',
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      attachment: {
        id: `att_${Date.now()}`,
        file_name: file.name,
        file_path: data.filePath,
        file_type: file.type,
      }
    };

    ws.current.send(JSON.stringify(message));
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, message]);
  };

  const handleSelectUser = async (users, groupName) => {
    const userIds = users.map(u => u.id);
    const res = await fetch('/api/conversations', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ userIds, name: groupName }),
    });
    const data = await res.json();

    if (data.isNew) {
      // In a real app, you'd probably want to refetch conversations here
      // For now, we'll just create a placeholder on the client
      const newClientConv = {
        conversation_id: data.conversation_id,
        user_id: userIds[0], // For simplicity, just use the first user for display
        user_name: groupName || users.map(u => u.name).join(', '),
        user_avatar: 'https://picsum.photos/seed/group/100',
        last_message_text: 'Started a new conversation',
        last_message_timestamp: Date.now(),
      };
      setConversations(prev => [newClientConv, ...prev]);
      setActiveConversation(newClientConv);
    } else {
      // Conversation already exists, find and activate it
      const existing = conversations.find(c => c.conversation_id === data.conversation_id);
      if (existing) {
        setActiveConversation(existing);
      }
    }

    setIsModalOpen(false);
  };

  const handleSearch = async (query) => {
    setSearchQuery(query);
    if (query.length > 2) {
      const res = await fetch(`/api/search/messages?query=${query}&userId=${currentUser.id}`);
      const data = await res.json();
      setSearchResults(data);
    } else {
      setSearchResults([]);
    }
  }

  const otherUser = activeConversation ? users[activeConversation.user_id] : null;

  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-slate-950 text-slate-200">
      {isModalOpen && <NewConversationModal users={users} onSelectUser={handleSelectUser} onClose={() => setIsModalOpen(false)} />}
      {/* Sidebar with conversation list */}
      <div className="w-1/4 border-r border-slate-800 flex flex-col">
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-slate-800 flex items-center gap-2">
          <button onClick={onBack} className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded-full">
            <ChevronLeft className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
          <h2 className="text-xl font-bold">NDOVERA Chat</h2>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="relative flex-1">
                <Search className="w-4 h-4 absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-500" />
                <input 
                  type="text" 
                  placeholder="Search messages..." 
                  className="pl-10 w-full bg-slate-800 border-none rounded-lg text-sm"
                  value={searchQuery}
                  onChange={(e) => handleSearch(e.target.value)}
                />
            </div>
            <button onClick={() => setIsModalOpen(true)} className="p-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-emerald-700">
              <Plus className="w-5 h-5" />
            </button>
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto">
          {searchQuery.length > 2 ? (
            searchResults.map(msg => (
              <div key={msg.id} className="p-4 border-b border-slate-800">
                <p className="text-sm font-bold">{msg.conversation_name || msg.sender_name}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-slate-400">{msg.text}</p>
              </div>
            ))
          ) : (
            conversations.map(conv => (
              <ConversationListItem 
                key={conv.conversation_id} 
                conversation={conv} 
                isActive={activeConversation?.conversation_id === conv.conversation_id}
                onClick={() => setActiveConversation(conv)}
              />
            ))
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Main chat window */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col">
        {activeConversation && otherUser ? (
          <>
            <div className="p-4 border-b border-slate-800 flex items-center gap-3">
                <img src={otherUser.avatarUrl} alt={otherUser.name} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/>
                <div>
                    <h3 className="font-bold text-slate-100">{otherUser.name}</h3>
                    {isTyping ? (
                      <p className="text-xs text-emerald-400 italic">typing...</p>
                    ) : (
                      <p className={`text-xs ${onlineUsers.has(otherUser.id) ? 'text-emerald-400' : 'text-slate-500'}`}>
                        {onlineUsers.has(otherUser.id) ? 'Online' : 'Offline'}
                      </p>
                    )}
                </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto flex flex-col-reverse">
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
                    {messages.map((msg) => (
                        <ChatMessage key={msg.id} message={msg} isYou={msg.sender_id === currentUser.id} users={users} currentUser={currentUser} />
                    ))}
                </div>
            </div>
            <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800">
                <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-lg flex items-center">
                    <input 
                      type="text" 
                      placeholder={`Message ${otherUser.name}...`} 
                      className="flex-1 bg-transparent border-none rounded-lg text-sm pl-4 py-3 focus:ring-0"
                      value={newMessage}
                      onChange={(e) => {
                        setNewMessage(e.target.value);
                        handleTyping(e.target.value.length > 0);
                      }}
                      onBlur={() => handleTyping(false)}
                      onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSendMessage()}
                    />
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-1 p-2">
                    <input type="file" id="file-upload" className="hidden" onChange={handleFileUpload} />
                    <label htmlFor="file-upload" className="p-2 text-slate-400 hover:text-white cursor-pointer"><Paperclip className="w-4 h-4"/></label>
                    <button onClick={handleSendMessage} className="p-2 bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-md hover:bg-emerald-700"><Send className="w-4 h-4"/></button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
          </>
        ) : (
          <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center text-slate-500">Select a conversation to start chatting</div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String: string) {
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - base64String.length % 4) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding)
    .replace(/-/g, '+')
    .replace(/_/g, '/');

  const rawData = window.atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);

  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) {
    outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  }
  return outputArray;
}

CODE 2: 
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { X } from 'lucide-react';

export default function NewConversationModal({ users, onSelectUser, onClose }) {
  const [selectedUsers, setSelectedUsers] = useState([]);
  const [groupName, setGroupName] = useState('');
  const currentUser = { id: 'user_teacher_1' }; // This would come from auth

  const handleUserSelect = (user) => {
    setSelectedUsers(prev => 
      prev.find(u => u.id === user.id) 
        ? prev.filter(u => u.id !== user.id) 
        : [...prev, user]
    );
  }

  const handleCreateConversation = () => {
    onSelectUser(selectedUsers, groupName);
  }

  return (
    <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-slate-900/80 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
      <div className="bg-slate-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl w-full max-w-md">
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-slate-700 flex justify-between items-center">
          <h3 className="font-bold text-lg">Start a New Conversation</h3>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-700 rounded-full">
            <X className="w-5 h-5" />
          </button>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4">
          {selectedUsers.length > 1 && (
            <input 
              type="text"
              placeholder="Group Name (optional)"
              value={groupName}
              onChange={(e) => setGroupName(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-slate-700 border-none rounded-lg text-sm mb-4"
            />
          )}
          <p className="text-sm text-slate-400 mb-4">Select one or more users to start chatting with:</p>
          <div className="max-h-80 overflow-y-auto">
            {Object.values(users).filter(user => user.id !== currentUser.id).map(user => (
              <button 
                key={user.id} 
                onClick={() => handleUserSelect(user)}
                className={`w-full text-left p-3 flex items-center gap-3 rounded-lg ${selectedUsers.find(u => u.id === user.id) ? 'bg-emerald-600/50' : 'hover:bg-slate-700/50'}`}
              >
                <img src={user.avatarUrl} alt={user.name} className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full" referrerPolicy="no-referrer"/>
                <div>
                  <p className="font-bold text-slate-200">{user.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">{user.role}</p>
                </div>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-700">
          <button 
            onClick={handleCreateConversation} 
            disabled={selectedUsers.length === 0}
            className="w-full bg-emerald-600 text-white rounded-lg py-2 disabled:bg-slate-600"
          >
            Start Conversation
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

To implement the **Light Mode** for the Ndovera project, we will follow the "Google AI Studio" aesthetic: clean, high-contrast, professional, and utilizing vibrant "Google-style" accent colours (Blue, Red, Yellow, Green).

Following the core architecture rules—**no file over 200 lines** and **feature isolation** —the Light Mode plan is broken down by system layer:

### 1. The Light Mode Palette (Theme Definitions)

Unlike the glassmorphic dark mode, the Light Mode uses a "Material Surface" approach with solid whites and soft greys to ensure maximum readability.

* **Backgrounds:** `bg-slate-50` (Page) and `bg-white` (Main Surface).
* **Typography:** `text-slate-900` (Headings) and `text-slate-600` (Body).
* **Borders:** `border-slate-200` (Clean, subtle separation).
* **Accent Colours:**
* **Primary (Blue):** `#1a73e8` (Google Blue) for primary actions.
* **Success (Green):** `text-emerald-700` / `bg-emerald-50` for active sidebar states.
* 
**Warning (Yellow):** For "Attention Required" status cards.


* 
**Danger (Red):** For "Urgent" or "Overdue" markers.





### 2. Colourful "Smart Card" System

Every dashboard summary will use the "StatsCard" component from `shared/components/`. In Light Mode, these cards will follow a vibrant, colour-coded logic:

* **Student Cards:**
* **Attendance:** Blue card with a soft shadow.
* 
**Recent Scores:** Green card (Positive) or Yellow (Needs work).


* 
**Farming Mode:** Purple card (Vibrant "Learning Economy" feel).




* **Parent/Accountant Cards:**
* 
**Paid Fees:** Bright Green card.


* 
**Outstanding Balance:** High-contrast Red card for urgency.


* 
**Scholarship/Waivers:** Sky Blue card.





### 3. Layout: Dual Scroll Logic

The sidebar and content area will maintain the independent scroll functionality you requested.

* **The Sidebar:** White background (`bg-white`) with a subtle right border (`border-r border-slate-200`).
* **The Active Item:** Uses `.sidebar-item-active` with `bg-emerald-50` background and a `border-r-4 border-emerald-600` for a clear, professional indicator.
* 
**The Scroll Reset:** Every click on a sidebar item will trigger a `window.scrollTo(0,0)` on the content container via a shared hook (`useDashboard.js`).



### 4. Role-Based Feature Implementation

The feature-specific components will adapt their UI to the Light Mode plan:

* 
**Classroom (Student):** Lesson notes will be displayed on clean white cards with "Google AI Studio" style colourful icons (e.g., Red for PDFs, Blue for Docs).


* 
**CBT & Exams (Security):** The interface will switch to a neutral, high-contrast white-and-grey layout to reduce eye strain and maximize focus during timed assessments.


* 
**ID Manager (Flip Card):** In Light Mode, the ID Card will look like a crisp, physical plastic card with a white front and a colourful back representing the "Switch Role" power.



### 5. Shared Design Assets (`shared/styles/theme.css`)

To maintain consistency across the entire project, all Light Mode styles must be defined globally:

```css
/* Shared Light Mode Theme Snippets */
.bg-primary-light { @apply bg-white border border-slate-200 shadow-sm; }
.text-header-light { @apply text-slate-900 font-semibold; }
.card-google-blue { @apply bg-blue-50 border-blue-100 text-blue-700; }
.card-google-green { @apply bg-emerald-50 border-emerald-100 text-emerald-700; }

```

This Light Mode plan ensures that while the **Night Mode** is futuristic and glassmorphic, the **Day Mode** is functional, vibrant, and optimized for administrative and academic productivity.

Got it! For **Ndovera Dark Mode**, a **premium, futuristic spinner** should feel **glassmorphic, neon-glowy, and smooth**, not the basic “loading circle.” Here’s a **modern spinner design** using **Tailwind CSS + optional keyframe animation**.

---

## **1. Glassmorphic Neon Spinner (Frosted Glow)**

```html
<div class="flex justify-center items-center h-screen bg-slate-950">
  <div class="w-16 h-16 border-4 border-t-emerald-400 border-cyan-500 border-b-violet-400 rounded-full animate-spin shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(0,255,255,0.4),0_0_25px_rgba(0,255,255,0.2)]"></div>
</div>
```

**Explanation:**

* `border-4` → thick ring for premium look
* `border-t-emerald-400 border-cyan-500 border-b-violet-400` → **multi-colored neon segments**
* `rounded-full` → perfect circle
* `animate-spin` → continuous smooth spin
* `shadow-[...]` → **futuristic neon glow effect**
* `bg-slate-950` → dark background for glass/neon contrast

✨ You can **increase size** (`w-24 h-24`) or **add extra rings** for depth.

---

## **2. Glass Layered Spinner (Frosted, Multi-layer)**

```html
<div class="flex justify-center items-center h-screen bg-slate-950">
  <div class="relative w-20 h-20 animate-spin">
    <div class="absolute inset-0 rounded-full border-4 border-t-emerald-400/50 border-cyan-500/50 backdrop-blur-xl shadow-xl"></div>
    <div class="absolute inset-2 rounded-full border-2 border-violet-400/70 animate-spin-reverse"></div>
  </div>
</div>
```

**Features:**

* Two layers spinning in **opposite directions** → premium futuristic effect
* Semi-transparent borders → glassmorphic feel
* Backdrop blur → subtle depth
* Neon accents → futuristic glow

**Add keyframes for reverse spin (Tailwind extend in `tailwind.config.js`):**

```js
module.exports = {
  theme: {
    extend: {
      animation: {
        'spin-reverse': 'spin-reverse 1s linear infinite',
      },
      keyframes: {
        'spin-reverse': {
          '0%': { transform: 'rotate(360deg)' },
          '100%': { transform: 'rotate(0deg)' },
        },
      },
    },
  },
};
```

Continuing the extraction and structuring of actionable requirements from NDOVERA.txt, here is the next section of the comprehensive, actionable to-do/specification guide, focusing on the Parent Dashboard and related features:

---

## Parent Dashboard: Actionable Specification Guide

### 1. Parent Dashboard Core
- [ ] Implement a dedicated Parent Dashboard, loaded automatically when the active role is "Parent".
- [ ] Ensure role switching via Smart ID Card for users with multiple roles (e.g., Parent + Teacher).
- [ ] Keep dashboards for different roles completely separated.

### 2. Sidebar Structure
- [ ] Implement sidebar navigation with the following sections:
  - Dashboard (Home Summary)
  - Children Switcher (Top Bar)
  - Academic Performance
  - Results
  - Assignments
  - Fees & Receipts
  - Tuck Shop
  - PTA Attendance
  - Messaging
  - Library
  - Auras Wallet
  - Profile & Security

### 3. Children Switcher (Core Engine)
- [ ] Place at the top of the dashboard (carousel or dropdown).
- [ ] Display for each child:
  - Name, Photo, School, Class & Arm, Status (Active/Inactive)
- [ ] Support multiple children, multiple schools, and different school sections.
- [ ] Allow parent to be staff (role switch).
- [ ] Only one child active at a time; switching refreshes dashboard instantly.
- [ ] Inactive child: view-only records, no live analytics, no new messages.
- [ ] If no active children: lock parent role (read-only archive access).

### 4. Dashboard (Home Summary)
- [ ] Display quick intelligence overview:
  - Current term summary, latest result average, attendance %, upcoming assignments, fee balance, recent messages, auras balance, alerts.
- [ ] No editing possible.

### 5. Academic Performance (Per Term Intelligence)
- [ ] Show subject performance overview, term comparison trends, improvement indicators (Improving, Stable, Needs Attention), teacher remarks.
- [ ] Use line graphs, color indicators, weak area flags.
- [ ] Parents cannot enter scores, adjust grading, or compare to other students.

### 6. Results (Official Records Tab)
- [ ] Scaffolded structure:
  - Level 1: Session Selector (newest session at top)
  - Level 2: Term Tabs inside session (newest term first)
- [ ] Each term displays:
  - Result summary card (overall average, grade, position, attendance %, promotion status, teacher/principal remark)
  - Subject breakdown table: | Subject | CA | Exam | Total | Grade | Remark |
  - Performance trend snapshot (mini graph)
- [ ] Fee gating logic: lock results if fees unpaid, show outstanding balance and "Pay Now" button, unlock on payment.
- [ ] All past results remain visible and archived; cannot be deleted by parent.

### 7. Assignments (Assist Mode)
- [ ] Parents can view assignment details, deadlines, submission status, teacher feedback, and help child offline.
- [ ] Parents cannot submit assignments, edit answers, upload files, or comment as student.

### 8. Fees & Receipts
- [ ] Show tuition, transport, extras, discounts, scholarships, outstanding balance.
- [ ] Payment flow: parent pays → HoS marks paid → system auto-generates receipt (stored, emailed, downloadable PDF).
- [ ] Parents cannot edit payment history.

### 9. Tuck Shop
- [ ] Show daily spending: item name, quantity, price, date/time, payment source.
- [ ] Credit system: parents can fund wallet, set spending limit.
- [ ] Parents cannot delete transactions or reverse payments.
- [ ] Receipts auto-issued when marked paid.

### 10. PTA Attendance (QR System)
- [ ] PTA generates QR code; parent scans at meeting.
- [ ] System logs date, time, event.
- [ ] Parents see attendance history and participation record.
- [ ] Parents cannot edit or manually mark attendance.

### 11. Messaging
- [ ] Structured, logged communication system.
- [ ] Parents can message class teacher, subject teachers, admin, support desk.
- [ ] Optional: student-to-student messaging disabled by default.
- [ ] All messages logged, moderated, reportable, non-anonymous.

### 12. Library
- [ ] Two layers:
  - School Library: assigned materials, read-only, encrypted, offline-capable.
  - Global Library (Premium): unlocked with Auras, parents can read/assign books to child, all content encrypted, app-only, non-exportable.

### 13. Auras Wallet
- [ ] Educational credit system.
- [ ] Parents can earn, purchase, transfer Auras to children, spend on Global Library, AI Analytics, premium features.
- [ ] Parents cannot withdraw cash, convert to money, or sell Auras.

### 14. AI Academic Insights (Premium)
- [ ] AI provides weak subject breakdown, performance pattern analysis, study plan recommendations, attendance-performance correlation, predictive alerts.
- [ ] Cannot modify grades, speak to teachers, or generate exam answers.

### 15. Profile & Security
- [ ] Show parent personal info, linked children, linked schools, roles (read-only).
- [ ] Security options: change password, enable 2FA, device history, session log.

### 16. Hard Permission Walls
- [ ] Parents can never: write exams, enter scores, modify attendance, grade assignments, override teachers, bypass fee gate, access other students’ data, escalate privileges, cash out Auras.

### 17. Edge Case Rules
- [ ] If child becomes inactive: live analytics stop, messaging disabled, results archived, library access limited.
- [ ] If parent has no active children: dashboard locks, archive access only.

---

- [ ] Student Management: View/transfer/inactivate students, track assignments/exams/results, set permissions, manage scholarships/badges.
- [ ] Staff Management: View/approve/terminate staff, assign roles, monitor load, AI-powered evaluations, export analytics, flag low performers, feedback templates.
- [ ] CA & Results Approval: Approve/sign/release results, audit logs, lock/unlock by fee status, archive results.
- [ ] Attendance & Analytics: Summaries, at-risk detection, teacher attendance, correlation charts, absentee alerts.
- [ ] Fees & Payments: Setup/override/track fees, auto-issue receipts, Auras payment integration, revenue analytics.
- [ ] Scholarships & Badges: Assign/manage scholarships/badges, rules for eligibility, track history, flag students.
- [ ] AI School Health Advisor: Monitors health, provides insights, suggests interventions, uses Auras for analytics.
- [ ] Reports & Exports: Weekly/monthly/termly reports, exportable, scheduled, customizable.
- [ ] Farming Mode/Auras Management: Enable/disable, cash-out, manage own Auras.
- [ ] Messaging: Broadcast, structured, logs/templates, chat with users/Ndovera HelpDesk, urgent alerts.
- [ ] Settings & Security: Configure policies, profile/password, audit log.
- [ ] Additional Advanced Features: Teacher evaluations, student analytics, exam/lesson plan oversight, integrated dashboard, fee/scholarship simulation.

### 4. Permissions & Rules
- [ ] HoS can: approve/sign/override results/fees, manage scholarships/badges, view analytics, cash-out Auras, approve plans/exams, manage question bank.
- [ ] HoS cannot: appoint another HoS, close school, transfer ownership.
- [ ] All actions logged for auditing.

### 5. ICT / System Admin Functions (HoS inherits ICT role)
- [ ] Network & System Health: Monitor servers, cloud, network, uptime, alerts.
- [ ] Device & User Management: Manage devices, assign/revoke access, usage logs, remote deactivation.
- [ ] System Configuration: Integrations (payments, AI, exams, library), adjust global settings.
- [ ] User Support & Issue Tracking: Manage support tickets, resolve/escalate, track SLA.
- [ ] Rules: HoS has full ICT control except owner-level tasks.

## Attendance Engine (Student & Staff)

### Student Attendance Engine

#### 1. Data Structure
- [ ] Fields: StudentID, ClassID, Date, MorningStatus, AfternoonStatus, MarkedBy, Role, Timestamp, Notes, ApprovalStatus.

#### 2. Role-Based Permissions
- [ ] Class Teacher: mark/override assigned class.
- [ ] Assistant: mark if delegated, limited override.
- [ ] HoS/Owner: mark/override any class.
- [ ] Temp Staff: mark if assigned.
- [ ] Regular Teacher: cannot mark unless elevated.
- [ ] Unauthorized attempts blocked/logged.

#### 3. Marking Engine Flow
- [ ] Role validation, class/date selection, mark sessions, save/submit, override with logging.

#### 4. Offline Support
- [ ] Download/upload CSV/JSON templates, validation engine for uploads, conflict resolution.

#### 5. Calculation Engine
- [ ] Status values: Present=1, Late=0.5, Absent=0, Excused=1.
- [ ] Daily points = Morning + Afternoon.
- [ ] Term % = (sum of daily points) / (2 × total days) × 100.
- [ ] Integrate with results, analytics, parent dashboard, HoS/Owner reports.

#### 6. Integration & Alerts
- [ ] Only approved entries count.
- [ ] Highlight low attendance, generate alerts, feed AI analytics.
- [ ] Parent dashboard: daily/term attendance, alerts, read-only for inactive students.
- [ ] Audit/logging: all actions, overrides flagged, audit reports.
- [ ] Notifications: parents (absent/late), class teacher (unmarked), HoS/Owner (trends).
- [ ] Special rules: inactive students not counted, excused absences configurable, students/parents cannot edit, temp staff assignments expire.

---

### Staff Attendance Engine

#### 1. Methods
- [ ] Mark via facial recognition, QR code, or device.
- [ ] Offline queueing, sync on reconnect, conflict resolution.

#### 2. Data Structure
- [ ] Fields: StaffID, Date, TimeIn, TimeOut, Method, DeviceID, Status, MarkedBy, Notes, PTAFlag.

#### 3. Role-Based Marking
- [ ] Staff: mark own attendance (face/QR).
- [ ] Admin/Security: mark any staff (device/manual).
- [ ] HoS/Owner: override/audit.
- [ ] Temp/Visitor: only if assigned, logged separately.
- [ ] Unauthorized attempts logged/flagged.

---

## Staff Attendance (continued)

- [ ] Notifications & alerts: Late/absent staff alerts, offline not synced reminders, PTA-linked staff notifications, weekly/termly security audit reports.

## PTA Attendance Engine

### 1. Attendance Method
- [ ] QR-based: Unique QR per PTA meeting/session, parents scan on arrival, logs ParentID, MeetingID, Timestamp, DeviceID; supports offline scan/queue.
- [ ] One scan per parent per meeting; multiple children handled automatically; invalid QR rejected/logged.

### 2. Data Structure
- [ ] Fields: ParentID, ChildrenIDs, MeetingID, Timestamp, DeviceID, Status (Present/Absent), Notes.

### 3. Dashboard & UI
- [ ] Admin/HoS/Owner: View attendees, search/filter, highlight absentees.
- [ ] Parent: Scan QR, view attendance history, notifications for meetings.

### 4. Offline Support
- [ ] Store scans locally, sync when online, flag conflicts.

### 5. Automatic Child Linkage
- [ ] Parents with children auto-linked; attendance counts for all children.

### 6. Printable/Exportable Reports
- [ ] PDF/CSV/Excel: Parent name, photo, children, contact, status, timestamp.

### 7. Analytics
- [ ] Attendance % per parent, event trends, flag consistent absentees, export summaries.

### 8. Security & Audit
- [ ] QR codes expire after meeting, log each scan, reject/flag duplicates, printable reports for compliance.

### 9. Workflow
- [ ] School creates meeting/QR, parent scans, system validates, logs attendance, admin/HoS/Owner can view/export/analyze.

- [ ] Workflow: Subject Teacher enters → Class Teacher reviews/overrides → Sectional Head reviews/comments → HoS final approval → System publishes (fee-gated if needed).
- [ ] Features: Spreadsheet upload, validation, audit logs, analytics, result integration, offline support, color-coded UI (overrides=yellow, returned=red, approved=green).

### Result Management System (RMS)
- [ ] Modules: CA Management, Exam Management (official), CBT Management (practice), Attendance Integration, Cognitive Card, Behavioral/Affective Card, Psychomotor Card, Grading Scale Management, Comments & Signatures, Watermark/Branding, Audit/Approval Workflow, Reports/Analytics, Dashboards, AI/Premium Features.
- [ ] Data Flow: CA entry → Exam scores → Class Teacher override → Sectional Head review → HoS approval → Result sheet calculation (cognitive, attendance, behavioral, psychomotor) → Dashboards/export.
- [ ] Result Sheet: Header (logo, term, session, student info), Cognitive Card (CA, Exam, Total, Position, Highest/Lowest, Avg, Grade, Remark), Behavioral/Affective Card (traits, rating), Psychomotor Card (height/weight), Comments & Signatures.
- [ ] Permissions: Role-based (Teacher, Class Teacher, Sectional Head, HoS, Proprietor), only HoS-approved grading scales/results visible, unapproved entries blocked.
- [ ] Integration: Student/Parent/Teacher/HoS/Proprietor dashboards, export with watermark, AI analytics, bulk printing.
- [ ] Premium: AI analytics, predictive alerts, trend comparison, customizable cards, bulk printing.

## Exam Tab (Official Exams)

### 1. Offline Exam Tab (Printable/Physical)
- [ ] Teachers set questions manually or upload formatted document (PDF/DOC).
- [ ] Question setting interface: class, subject, term, session, duration, total marks, instructions, objective/theory questions.
- [ ] Exam body format: auto-generated header (logo, school, term, subject, etc.), two-column layout for objectives, theory at end, professional print format.
- [ ] Approval workflow: Teacher → Sectional Head → HoS (final approval, lock for printing, all changes logged).
- [ ] Score entry: After marking, scores entered manually via CA Score Sheet (Exam column).

### 2. Online Exam Tab (Official Digital Exam)
- [ ] Students take official exams online; scores flow into CA Score Sheet.
- [ ] Supported question types: MCQ, True/False, Fill in the Blank, Short Answer, Structured Response, Essay, Matching, Case Study, Diagram labeling.
- [ ] Strictness features: timer lock, anti-tab switch, full screen, randomization, question pooling, IP/device logging, webcam proctoring (premium), attempt limit, auto-save, plagiarism detection.
- [ ] Workflow: Teacher creates → Sectional Head preview → HoS approves → scheduled for students → students take exam → auto/manual grading → scores captured in CA Score Sheet.
- [ ] Result integration: Online exam scores auto-inserted into CA Score Sheet, Cognitive Card, total, grade, class position.
- [ ] Both offline and online require HoS-approved setup.

---

## Question Bank & Deduplication

### 1. Deduplication Flow
- [ ] Normalize question text (lowercase, remove punctuation, spaces, symbols, numbering, formatting).
- [ ] Hashing: SHA-256 for question/options, block exact matches.
- [ ] Semantic similarity: token overlap, n-grams, subject/topic/exam type, flag/review/accept based on similarity.
- [ ] Answer consistency: compare answers for similar questions, admin review if conflict.
- [ ] Deduplication decision table: block, flag, review, accept.

### 2. Database Schema
- [ ] questions: id, question_text, normalized_text, question_hash, subject_id, topic_id, exam_type, difficulty, source, status, created_by, approved_by, created_at, updated_at.
- [ ] question_options: id, question_id, option_text, normalized_text, is_correct.
- [ ] question_answers: id, question_id, answer_text, source, verified, verified_by, locked, created_at.
- [ ] question_usage: question_id, used_in, tenant_id, times_used.
- [ ] question_audit_logs: action, question_id, user_id, old_value, new_value, timestamp.

### 3. Approval & Override Workflow
- [ ] Teacher creates/edits drafts → system deduplication → draft → Sectional Head review → HoS approval → approved/active.
- [ ] Roles: Teacher (draft), Sectional Head (review), HoS (final approval/lock), Proprietor (override), Ami (global override).
- [ ] Overrides: logged, versioned, non-destructive, old versions retained.

### 4. Question Reuse Mapping
- [ ] Single source of truth: every question exists once, referenced by CBT, Exam, Assignment.
- [ ] Engine behavior flags: CBT (practice, no result impact), Online Exam (timed, strict, result impact), Offline Exam (physical, result impact), Assignment (homework/classwork, result impact).
- [ ] Data flow: Question Bank → CBT/Exam/Assignment (no duplication, no AI repeat calls).

---

## Fees Engine (start)

### 1. Core Financial Principles
- [ ] Fees are per child, not per class.
- [ ] Results locked if fees outstanding.
- [ ] HoS/Owner controls fees by default.
- [ ] Accountant sees revenue, not fee policy (unless permitted).
- [ ] Receipts are proof of payment.
- [ ] Every transaction is auditable and reversible (not deletable).

### 2. Fee Structure Management
- [ ] HoS/Owner: full fee control; Accountant: no control unless permitted; Ami: emergency override.
- [ ] Fee components per child: tuition, extra care, welfare, custom items (transport, feeding, books, uniform, etc.), each with amount, term applicability, mandatory/optional flag.
- [ ] Calculation engine: Total Expected = sum of all items; Final Payable = Total Expected - scholarships - discounts; recalculates on badge/payment/fee item change.

### 3. Badges & Automatic Discounts
- [ ] Scholarship badge: 100% or partial waiver, item-specific.
- [ ] Staff child badge: predefined discount rules, can exclude items.

## Fees Engine (continued)

- [ ] Payment modes: installment, bulk.
- [ ] Manual confirmation by Accountant (current), payment gateway/auto-confirmation (future).
- [ ] Historic payment confirmation: lookup by receipt number, shows student, items, amount, date, confirmer, source.
- [ ] Auto balance update: Outstanding Balance = Final Payable - Total Paid; status auto-updates (Paid/Partial/Owing).

### 3. Receipts System
- [ ] Auto-generate receipt on payment (unique number, PDF, logo, watermark, student, term/session).
- [ ] Stored permanently, appears in Parent Dashboard, downloadable anytime.
- [ ] Receipts cannot be edited or deleted.

### 4. Result Access Lock Engine
- [ ] If outstanding balance > 0: results locked, parent sees amount owed and "Pay now".
- [ ] Once cleared: results unlock automatically.

### 5. Auto Fee Reminder Engine
- [ ] Triggers: X days before deadline, on partial payment, on overdue.
- [ ] Channels: in-app, email, SMS (optional).
- [ ] Recipients: parent, HoS, accountant (summary).

### 6. Accountant Dashboard (Limited)

- [ ] Accountant cannot: modify fees, apply discounts, override balances, unlock results.

- [ ] Tables: student_fees, fee_items, payments, receipts, badges, audit_logs.

### 8. Financial Security Model
- [ ] RBAC, dual approval for overrides/badge removal, immutable logs, receipt verification, no hard deletes, session-based checks.

### 9. Parent Payment Experience (UI)
- [ ] View breakdown, discounts, balance; pay (installment/bulk); instant status/receipt; results unlock if cleared.

### 10. Revenue Analytics Engine
- [ ] Metrics: expected vs collected, category performance, discount impact, risk index, term comparison.
- [ ] Dashboards: HoS, Owner, Ami.

### 11. Multi-Campus/Multi-Tenant
- [ ] Each campus: own fee structure/accounts, group-level reporting, no data leakage.

### 12. Term-Based Fee Duplication
- [ ] Copy/modify last term’s structure, preserve history.

### 13. Revenue Forecasting AI (future)
- [ ] Inputs: enrollment, payment, discount, dropout; outputs: cashflow, risk, budget.

### 14. Final Guarantees
- [ ] Per-child model, receipt verification, locked results on debt, reminders, controlled permissions, audit-safe, scalable.

## NDOVERA Library System

### 1. Library Modes
- [ ] Physical Library: traditional borrowing, offline allowed, librarian confirms returns.
- [ ] Digital Reading: in-app only, paid/free, no download.
- [ ] User-Submitted Digital Library: users upload, others read for a fee, revenue split (80% owner, 20% NDOVERA).
- [ ] Multi-School Shared Library: shared question banks, books, materials, permissions per school.

### 2. User Roles & Visibility
- [ ] Students, parents, teachers, librarians, contributors, admin: each with specific access (read, borrow, upload, manage, recommend, earnings).

### 3. Book Types
- [ ] Textbooks, storybooks, revision guides, past questions, research, novels, etc.

### 4. Pricing & Aura System
- [ ] Book price in Naira, system auto-calculates Aura equivalent, free books allowed.

### 5. Revenue Sharing
- [ ] Per read/borrow, not upload; tracked and split.

### 6. Book Submission Pipeline
- [ ] Upload → AI quality analysis (readability, plagiarism, structure, relevance) → AI generates summary/tags/pricing → admin review → approval/rejection → publish.

### 7. Borrowing System (Physical)
- [ ] Borrow by student/staff ID, offline supported, librarian confirms returns.

### 8. Digital Reading Engine
- [ ] In-app reader, page/time tracking, bookmarking, watermark, copy prevention.

### 9. History & Transparency
- [ ] Borrow/read history visible to student, parent, librarian, contributor (earnings only).

### 10. Security & Rights
- [ ] No download (unless admin), DRM, user watermark, session-based, abuse detection, encrypted books.

### 11. Payments & Earnings
- [ ] Contributor wallet, Aura/naira balance, withdrawal rules, account details.

### 12. Offline Borrowing Support
- [ ] Librarian logs offline borrow, syncs later, flags unreturned items.

### 13. Multi-School Tenant Control
- [ ] Each school can enable/disable digital/paid library, NDOVERA global content optional.

### 14. Library Analytics Dashboard
- [ ] Librarian: most borrowed, overdue, trends. Admin: revenue, content quality, contributor performance.

### 15. Database Schema
- [ ] Tables: library_books, book_versions, book_categories, book_pricing, physical_borrows, digital_reads, return_confirmations, library_transactions, aura_wallets, earnings_split, ai_analysis_reports, admin_reviews, content_flags.

### 16. Audit & Compliance
- [ ] Track uploads, approvals, pricing edits, revenue logs (immutable).

### 17. Integration
- [ ] Finance (Aura↔₦), parent app (history), student dashboard (reading), admin panel (moderation), CBT/assignment (reference).

---

## Farming Mode (Educators Appreciation)

### 1. Basics
- [ ] Optional activation, ads integrated (not during assignments/exams), appears in lesson notes, library, dashboard, AI, CBT.
- [ ] Auras earned for engagement (lessons, reading, assignments, CBT).
- [ ] Display: coins, badges, points on dashboard; users see only Auras.

### 2. Cashout Rules
- [ ] Staff: eligible after 2 months, must withdraw within 7 days or reset.
- [ ] Parents/students: cannot withdraw, can spend in-app, Auras reset every 3 months if unused.

### 3. Backend
- [ ] Tables: farming_mode_config, auras_transactions, auras_balance, auras_reset_schedule, auras_cashout_log.
- [ ] No manual balance modification, logs immutable, admin/HoS can view but not alter balances.

### 4. User Experience
- [ ] Staff: dashboard shows balance, cashout when eligible, enter payment details, transaction logged.
- [ ] Students/parents: dashboard shows balance, spend on allowed features, receive reset alerts.

### 5. Notifications & Analytics
- [ ] Reminders for cashout/reset, analytics for admin/owner/HoS (total earned/spent, unclaimed, engagement impact).

### 6. Integration
- [ ] Student/parent/teacher dashboards, library, AI Tutor, ads engine.

## AI Systems

### 1. AI School Health Advisor (Staff)
- [ ] Attendance trends, result-attendance correlation, fee default prediction (paid), workload insights (paid), student risk alerts.
- [ ] Aura cost per report set by Super Admin, spending triggers transaction log.

### 2. AI Tutor (Student)
- [ ] Homework help, lesson explanations, exam prep (all paid in Auras, cost set by Super Admin), free basic help allowed.

### 3. Teacher AI Assistance
- [ ] Lesson planning, material suggestions, class summaries/reports (all paid in Auras).

### 4. Super Admin Control
- [ ] Aura pricing management, monitoring, transparency, audit compliance.

### 5. User Flow
- [ ] Staff/teachers: see features/cost, spend Auras, access report/plan, transaction logged.
- [ ] Students: select AI Tutor feature, spend Auras, receive help, dashboard updates.

## Analytics & Reports

### 1. Tenant School Analytics
- [ ] Accessible to Owner/HoS/Principal (own school only).
- [ ] Reports: active/inactive students, attendance trends, fee outstanding, academic performance, exportable (PDF/Excel), logo/name/date/formatting.
- [ ] Data isolation: cannot see other schools, cannot modify history, no Ndovera-wide stats.

### 2. NDOVERA Global Analytics (Super Admin)
- [ ] Only aggregated stats: schools onboarded, active students, staff, farming mode, Auras, AI, website builder, revenue.
- [ ] No individual student/parent/grade/fee data.
- [ ] Smart dashboard: real-time widgets, graphs, filters (date, class, term, session, subject).
- [ ] Backend tables: analytics_student_status, analytics_attendance, analytics_fees, analytics_academic, analytics_exports, global_analytics.

---

## Security & Governance

### 1. Strict RBAC
- [ ] Permission-based actions, roles: Super Admin, Owner, HoS, Principal, Head Teacher, Teacher, ICT, Parent, Student.
- [ ] UI/API/DB guards, no hidden privileges, no auto-inheritance.

### 2. Hard Tenant Data Isolation
- [ ] Every record tagged with school_id, queries scoped, media per-school, no cross-school joins.

### 3. Immutable Audit Logs
- [ ] Log: account creation, role change, edits, Auras, cashout, AI, website, login printing.
- [ ] Logs: append-only, timestamped, non-editable, visible to governance roles, not deletable (even by Super Admin).

### 4. Super Admin Privacy
- [ ] Can: enable/suspend schools, view aggregated stats, manage templates, configure pricing.
- [ ] Cannot: view student names, parent contacts, grades, fee records, credentials, impersonate users.

---

## NDOVERA Identity System

### 1. ID Formats
- [ ] Student: NL-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
- [ ] Staff: NS-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
- [ ] Parent: NP-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}
- [ ] IDs: auto-generated, immutable, unique per school, never recycled, visible in place of sensitive data.

### 2. Email Structure
- [ ] Internal format: username@schoolname.com, displayed as masked (jo***@schoolname.com), never exposes personal emails, internal routing only, not editable, used for notifications.

## Printing Login Details

### 1. Permissions & Timing
- [ ] Only HoS/ICT Officer can print login details (never teachers, parents, students, Super Admin).
- [ ] Only during onboarding, for users with temporary password and who have never logged in.

### 2. Print Content & Security
- [ ] Print: Public ID, system email, temp password, role, login URL.
- [ ] One-time visibility: temp password visible once, deleted after first login, cannot be reprinted.
- [ ] Print token required, expires in minutes.
- [ ] Temp password expires if not used in X days.
- [ ] Audit log: who printed, role, school, count, timestamp, device/IP.
- [ ] A4 format: header, table, footer, watermark, page numbering, tracking ID.
- [ ] Prohibited: no reprint after login, no Excel export, no plain password email, no Super Admin access, no bypass of logs.

---

## Alumni Module

### 1. ID & Email
- [ ] Alumni: NA-{SCHOOL_INITIALS}-{000001}, email: jo***@alumni.schoolname.com, linked to original student ID, system-generated, masked, secure password only.

### 2. Onboarding
- [ ] HoS/ICT converts graduates, system generates ID/email/temp password, login details via controlled print/email, one-time, audit logged.
- [ ] Optional self-onboarding: alumni claim account, set password, update profile, all updates logged.

### 3. Dashboard & Features
- [ ] Profile, graduation year, event notifications, news, alumni network/forums, donation/paid courses (if enabled).

### 4. RBAC & Analytics
- [ ] Alumni: limited permissions, read-only on student/teacher data, can join events/discussions, all actions audited.
- [ ] Analytics: participation, event attendance, donations, graduation trends, newsletter engagement.

### 5. Printing Alumni Login
- [ ] Same as students: one-time, audit logged, temp password expires after first login.

### 6. Monetization
- [ ] Premium content/events/courses, Aura price set by Super Admin/Owner.

---

## Super Admin (Ami) Blueprint

### 1. Core Philosophy & Access
- [ ] Modular, independent backend ("Vault"), lazy-loaded frontend, security-by-design, unconventional terms for security.

### 2. Authentication
- [ ] Gatekeeper handles sessions, JWT+HMAC+refresh, MFA mandatory, RBAC (AmiMaster, AmiObserver, AmiOperator), AES-256 encrypted tokens.

### 3. Frontend/Backend Structure
- [ ] Lazy-loaded React modules: Colony (tenant mgmt), Blueprint (templates), AuricVault (pricing), Spectrometer (analytics), Sentinel (audit), Oracle (AI), PortalForge (website), Cipher (user mgmt), Rampart (security).
- [ ] Backend: Node.js/NestJS, PostgreSQL (row-level security, encryption), Redis, Nginx+WAF, rate-limiting, IP whitelisting, geo-blocking, two DBs (mainDB, vaultDB).

### 4. Security & Obfuscation
- [ ] Obfuscated table/field names, append-only logs, SSO+MFA, rate limiting, sharding/geo-redundancy.

### 5. Features Summary
- [ ] Tenant mgmt, template control, pricing, analytics, audit, AI oversight, website deployment, secure login printing, ID/email mgmt, flexible scaling.

---

## Messaging & Question Bank System (start)

### 1. Messaging System
- [ ] WhatsApp-like, real-time, file/voice/image sharing, read receipts, typing, role-based contact visibility, auditable.
- [ ] Contact visibility: parents (only their children’s teachers/admins), teachers (students/parents they teach, other teachers/admins), students (their teachers/class teacher/announcements), admin/owner/HoS (everyone).
- [ ] Chat types: one-to-one (parent-teacher, student-teacher, staff-staff), group (class, subject, staff, management), official channels (announcements, exam notices).
- [ ] Only admins can create sensitive groups, group membership auto-updated.

## Messaging System (continued)

### 1. Features
- [ ] WhatsApp-level: text, emojis, voice notes, images, PDFs, replies, restricted forwarding, search, delete (with audit).
- [ ] No anonymous users; all messages linked to real roles.
- [ ] Admin visibility for dispute resolution; deleted messages logged.
- [ ] No external contacts; fully internal NDOVERA network.
- [ ] Offline-first: messages can be typed offline, stored locally, auto-sent when online, graceful sync conflict handling.

---

## Question Bank System

### 1. Purpose & Uniqueness
- [ ] Global, duplicate-safe, non-AI; only teacher-created or assignment-derived questions.
- [ ] Automatically collects questions, prevents duplicates, class/subject-based, available across NDOVERA, teacher-controlled usage.

### 2. Sources
- [ ] Assignments (homework, classwork, tests, exams).
- [ ] Manual uploads (PDF/typed by teachers, parsed and stored).

### 3. Deduplication
- [ ] System checks text similarity, subject, class, topic, keywords.
- [ ] If match: link, don’t duplicate; if new: store as canonical.

### 4. Structure
- [ ] Each question: questionId, subject, class, topic, questionText, options, answer, difficulty, source, createdBy, usageCount.

### 5. Access & Governance
- [ ] Teachers: add/use, not edit/delete; HoD/Admin: use only; NDOVERA system: add only.
- [ ] Questions are permanent, history preserved, academic integrity maintained.
- [ ] Teachers see questions for their subject/class; schools can reuse but not edit others’ questions; usage count increases globally.

### 6. Use Cases
- [ ] Setting assignments, building tests/exams, revision, randomized practice, standardized assessments.

### 7. Messaging + Question Bank Link
- [ ] Assignments auto-add questions to bank; teacher sends assignment link via chat; parent notified; student submits; system learns (no AI).

---

- [ ] Communication is controlled, fast, and safe.
- [ ] Parents only see what they should; teachers save time.
- [ ] Questions never get lost; academic quality improves yearly.
- [ ] NDOVERA becomes smarter without AI abuse.

User: This specific error, "Failed to load module script: Expected a JavaScript-or-Wasm module script but the server responded with a MIME type of 'text/html'", usually occurs in React/Vite projects when the browser requests a .tsx or .js file, but the server cannot find it and returns your index.html file instead.Based on the NDOVERA system architecture and standard Vite configurations, here is how to troubleshoot and fix this bit-by-bit:1. Check the index.html Script PathIn a standard Vite project (like the one outlined in the NDOVERA blueprint), your index.html should be in the root directory and point correctly to your entry point.The Issue: If your script tag looks like <script type="module" src="main.tsx"></script>, but your entry file is actually at src/index.jsx (as specified in the NDOVERA structure), the server fails to find main.tsx and serves the HTML "404" page instead.The Fix: Ensure the src attribute in your index.html matches the file location in your src/ folder:HTML<script type="module" src="/src/index.jsx"></script>
2. Verify Case Sensitivity (Strict Naming)The NDOVERA blueprint enforces Strict Naming Conventions.The Issue: If your file is named Main.tsx (PascalCase) but your code imports /src/main.tsx (lowercase), Linux-based servers or build tools will fail to find the file and return a text/html error.The Fix: Ensure every import and script reference exactly matches the filename casing:Components: PascalCase.jsx.Hooks/Services: camelCase.js.3. Check Base URL in vite.config.jsIf you are deploying the dashboard to a subfolder (e.g., yoursite.com/dashboard/), the browser might look for the modules in the wrong place.The Fix: Open your vite.config.js and ensure the base property is set correctly:JavaScriptexport default defineConfig({
  base: '/', // Use './' if deploying to a relative subfolder
  // ... rest of config
});
4. Feature Isolation Import ErrorsThe NDOVERA "Import Rule" states that you should never deep-import from internal feature folders.The Issue: Using import { X } from '../../features/auth/components/LoginForm' can sometimes lead to resolution errors if the path is slightly off.The Fix: Use the index.js pattern required by the blueprint:Ensure src/features/dashboard/index.js exports your components.Use the alias: import { DashboardPage } from '@/features/dashboard'.5. Clear Build CacheSometimes the Vite transformation cache gets corrupted, causing it to serve raw files that the browser interprets as HTML.The Fix:Stop your development server.Delete the node_modules/.vite folder.Restart with npm run dev.Summary Checklist for NDOVERA Structure:File to CheckBlueprint RequirementPotential Errorindex.htmlScript must point to src/index.jsx.Pointing to main.tsx (missing file).Project RootOne feature = one folder.Misplaced files in root instead of features/.ImportsNo file > 200 lines.Overstuffed files causing compilation timeouts.MIME TypeServer must send application/javascript.Server sending index.html for missing files.

GitHub Copilot: Read [](file:///c%3A/Users/HP/Documents/ndovera/frontend/package.json)

Read [](file:///c%3A/Users/HP/Documents/ndovera/frontend/src/index.jsx)

The MIME-type error means the browser requested a module (like `/src/main.tsx`) but the dev server returned HTML (usually index.html). Here’s how to fix it in this NDOVERA CRA project:

- **Entry script:** CRA doesn’t use a `<script type="module">` tag in index.html, so this error generally happens only when the browser is pointed at a Vite-style HTML file (with `<script type="module" src="/src/main.jsx"></script>`). Make sure you’re starting the CRA dev server via `npm start` and visiting the URL it prints (`http://localhost:3000`). Don’t open index.html directly or copy over a Vite HTML template.

- **File paths/casing:** Ensure the entry file the dev server builds from actually exists. CRA expects index.js. You also have index.jsx; keep only one entry file (prefer the CRA default index.js) and delete/rename duplicates to avoid confused imports, then restart `npm start`.

- **Vite config:** There’s no [vite.config.js] in this repo because it’s CRA-based. If you meant to run Vite, you need to migrate the project (create `vite.config.js`, update index.html, etc.). Otherwise stick with CRA scripts.

- **Module imports:** The NDOVERA blueprint prefers re-export files. Ensure every `import` points to an actual file and respects casing (e.g., DashboardHome.jsx vs `dashboardHome.jsx`). A mismatched case on a case-sensitive FS will trigger this error.

- **Cache reset:** Stop the CRA server, delete .cache, then `npm start` again to clear stale module paths.

Once you align the entry file and ensure the CRA dev server is serving the app, that MIME-type error will disappear.

User: Check this to update the dark mode
Here is a breakdown of the visual language used in the app:
1. Color Palette & Depth
Deep Space Foundation: The app uses a "Dark Mode" base with a radial gradient background (#020617 to #0f172a). This creates a sense of depth and focus, making interactive elements "pop."
Functional Accents:
Indigo/Violet: Used for primary institutional actions and branding.
Emerald: Signals growth, wealth (Lams), and success.
Amber: Reserved for reminders, warnings, and "draft" states.
Rose: Exclusively used for "Live" states and critical alerts.
Subtle Borders: Instead of solid lines, it uses low-opacity borders (border-white/5 or border-indigo-500/20) to define shapes without creating visual clutter.
2. Typography & Hierarchy
Aggressive Weight: Headings use font-black with tracking-tighter for a bold, authoritative "Command Center" feel.
Micro-Labels: The UI is filled with tiny, uppercase labels (often text-[8px] or text-[10px]) with wide letter-spacing (tracking-widest). This mimics the look of high-end technical equipment or scientific instruments.
Monospace Accents: While the primary font is a clean sans-serif, numeric data and status codes are treated with a precision-focused layout that emphasizes scannability.
3. Shapes & Surfaces
Hyper-Rounded Corners: The app uses oversized border radii (rounded-[40px] or rounded-3xl). This softens the "cold" technical feel, making the "Nation-State" interface feel modern and approachable.
Glassmorphism: Many panels use backdrop-blur-3xl and semi-transparent backgrounds (bg-slate-950/80). This creates a layered UI where content feels like it's floating on glass screens.
Bento Grid Layout: Information is organized into "cells" of varying sizes, creating a rhythmic and organized structure that handles dense information well.
4. Interaction & Motion
Atmospheric Entry: Components use "Slam-in" or "Fade-in" animations (animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-bottom-4) to make the interface feel alive as you navigate.
Active Feedback: Buttons often feature a group-hover:scale-125 effect on icons and subtle glow transitions, providing clear tactile feedback.
Live Indicators: The use of animate-ping on status dots provides a constant sense of "real-time" synchronization with the "Node."
Summary Mood
The styling communicates "Institutional Intelligence." It feels like a sovereign, zero-trust operating system where every pixel is intentional, designed for a user who is a "Master" of their educational workspace.

GitHub Copilot: I’ll align your dark mode to this “Institutional Intelligence” visual language by updating the theme tokens (palette, depth, borders, typography classes) and then applying them to the dashboard surfaces/components so the look changes immediately. NDOVERA CLASSROOM — MOBILE EXPERIENCE

Focused. Full-screen. Zero distraction.

On mobile, Ndovera Classroom is designed to feel like entering a real classroom — once inside, nothing else competes for attention.

🚪 ENTERING THE CLASSROOM (Mobile Flow)
📌 Classroom Tab (Sidebar → Mobile)

On mobile, the sidebar collapses into a bottom navigation bar

Tapping Classroom:

Takes over the entire screen

Hides the main dashboard completely

Activates Classroom Mode

🔙 A Home / Back button appears at the top-left
This is the only way to exit the classroom and return to the main dashboard.

✅ This creates a strong mental boundary:
Dashboard = management
Classroom = learning

🧭 MOBILE BOTTOM NAVIGATION (Inside Classroom)

Once inside the classroom, the bottom nav switches to class-specific navigation.

📍 Bottom Navigation Tabs

Home

Classroom overview

Recent announcements

Today’s tasks

Quick status (due, overdue, completed)

Tasks

All assignments, tests, materials, practices

Grouped by:

Week

Topic

Scheme of Work

Expand / collapse sections for cleanliness

Stream

Noticeboard / Class announcements

Pinned rules stay at the top

Student announcements appear only if teacher permits

Members

Students list (read-only for students)

Teacher list

Status indicators (active, muted, flagged)

More

Classroom info

Class rules

Resources

Exit Classroom (same as back/home)

📢 NOTICEBOARD ON MOBILE (Stream Tab)
👩‍🏫 Teacher Powers

Post announcements

Pin messages

Share files, videos, links

Enable or disable comments

Enable or disable student announcements

🎓 Student Permissions (If Allowed)

Students may:

Post announcements (clearly labeled as Student Post)

Comment respectfully

Ask class-wide questions

Students may NOT:

Spam

Flood the stream

Override pinned teacher posts

🚨 Teachers can revoke posting rights instantly.

🧠 TASK EXPERIENCE (Mobile-First)
📂 My Tasks View

Clean card-based layout

Each task shows:

Type (color-coded)

Due date

Status (pending / submitted / returned)

📝 Task Workspace (Full Screen)

When a task opens:

It becomes a private, distraction-free workspace

No notifications

No side menus

Auto-save enabled

📌 Floating buttons:

Ask Teacher

Submit

Save Draft

💬 PRIVATE HELP CHAT (Mobile)

Inside each task:

A dedicated 1-on-1 chat

Only student + teacher

Appears as a slide-up panel

Can be minimized while working

🧠 Encourages shy students to ask questions confidently.

🔁 RESUBMISSION FLOW (Mobile)

If work is returned:

Task status changes to “Needs Improvement”

Teacher comments appear clearly

Student taps Improve & Resubmit

Previous version is preserved (no loss of work)

🎨 MOBILE THEMES
☀ Light Mode — Ndovera Studio (Mobile)

White background

Large readable text

Clear icons

Perfect for daylight and school environments

🌙 Night Mode — Ndovera Glass (Mobile)

Dark, glassmorphic cards

Soft glow borders

Frosted panels

Reduced eye strain

Feels premium and futuristic

🧩 DESIGN PHILOSOPHY (Mobile)

One screen = one purpose

No clutter

No noise

No confusion

When students are in the classroom,
they are mentally “in class.”

⭐ FINAL MOBILE SUMMARY

✔ Bottom navigation replaces sidebar
✔ Classroom tab takes full screen
✔ Home/Back button exits classroom
✔ Teacher-controlled announcements
✔ Student posts only when permitted
✔ Private, focused task workspace
✔ Premium light & glass night modes

Ndovera Classroom on mobile feels intentional, calm, and powerful.
Not just an app — a digital learning environment 🚀

✅ FINAL NOTE
✅ FINAL NOTE
This blueprint represents the complete NDOVERA School System — a future-ready education platform intentionally designed to:
•	📈 Scale nationally across thousands of schools
•	📴 Work offline-first, supporting low-connectivity environments
•	🔐 Protect data by design with strict security and governance
•	👩‍🏫 Empower educators through automation, AI, and clarity
•	🏫 Simplify school operations without compromising control or compliance
At its core, NDOVERA is not just software — it is a secure digital foundation for modern education systems, built to earn trust, reduce complexity, and unlock sustainable growth for schools, educators, and learners alike.
